
-----title
慈溪 (出生地)
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年1月2日</a>　此日，先生生。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='61b3ef0058cb4a3980eaa319fa7d2167_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("61b3ef0058cb4a3980eaa319fa7d2167");'><span id='61b3ef0058cb4a3980eaa319fa7d2167_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1160')">1148-1160年</a>，8-20岁</div><div id='61b3ef0058cb4a3980eaa319fa7d2167' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年</a>　入小学，便俨立若成人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　既长，任干蛊，主出入家用外，终日侍通奉公旁。为文清润峻整，务明圣经，不肯规时好作俗下语。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e322f1cbdfe64d08b294be4b18999403_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e322f1cbdfe64d08b294be4b18999403");'><span id='e322f1cbdfe64d08b294be4b18999403_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>，22岁</div><div id='e322f1cbdfe64d08b294be4b18999403' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1162&endYear=1162')">1162年</a>　绍兴末，虏突进淮右，考庭显避地慈溪，因占籍焉。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6359897b51d74f049a22eceab6562d65_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6359897b51d74f049a22eceab6562d65");'><span id='6359897b51d74f049a22eceab6562d65_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>，48岁</div><div id='6359897b51d74f049a22eceab6562d65' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年11月29日</a>　此日，葬父于县之石台乡句余村孝顺里。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='28cbefc7ce3249af8594de05284c8a33_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("28cbefc7ce3249af8594de05284c8a33");'><span id='28cbefc7ce3249af8594de05284c8a33_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1198')">1196-1198年</a>，56-58岁</div><div id='28cbefc7ce3249af8594de05284c8a33' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　先生归自胄监，家食者十四载。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　张渭兄弟访先生，与之交，姑系于本年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年立秋</a>　立秋，记磬斋。作品：《记》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明记文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年8月</a>　是月，撰《东山赋》<div id='poem_1282074' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282074' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282074?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东山赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282074")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282074_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282074'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282074'>吾之日用何如哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282074_comment'></div>如东山之晓色，苍茫无际，不可揽取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282074_comment'></div>其间云气隐见，阳辉粲发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282074_comment'></div>霞舒金锦，愈变而愈奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282074_comment'></div>云拖玉龙，出没夭娇于万峰群翠之间，可观可骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282074_comment'></div>而须臾忽化千态万状，莫绘莫画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282074_comment'></div>又如江上之秋光，清空爽明，若甚近也而不可执，若远也而不可追而及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282074_comment'></div>清露濡之，霜月炯之，而无所损、无所益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282074_comment'></div>又如松间之溪声，玲玲其鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282074_comment'></div>其音甚清，的然可以听而闻，而不得夫音之形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282074_comment'></div>又如岩前之月明，其洁如玉，其流光凝止，若可以敛而掬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282074_comment'></div>入松为松，入竹为竹，随物赋形，而终不得其机轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282074_comment'></div>此岂吾之所私有，独妙独化，他人不得而与哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282074_comment'></div>举遐近，通万古，夫孰者之不然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282074_comment'></div>惟昏明之不齐，是非之迭出，所以有知有不知，有协于极、于不极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282074_comment'></div>粒我烝民，莫非尔极，孰谓吾日用而非极乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282074_comment'></div>孰谓吾日用而可以知、可以识乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282074_comment'></div>孔子曰：「哀乐相生」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282074_comment'></div>正明目而视之不可得而见也，倾耳而听之不可得而闻也，孰谓吾日用而可以见、而可以闻乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282074_comment'></div>偶书如右，他日名之曰《东山赋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282074_comment'></div>或疑当名《日用赋》，应之曰：「如此问，不惟不识东山，亦不识日用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282074_comment'></div>庆元丙辰仲秋，书于石鱼竹房。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1282074_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年11月13日</a>　十一月十三日，过庭书训付恪。记连理瑞。作品：《记》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明记文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年12月27日</a>　赵师郑妻陈夫人葬于此日，为撰墓志铭。作品：《志》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明志文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　撰《广居赋》，姑系于本年。<div id='poem_1282072' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282072' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282072?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广居赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282072")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282072_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282072'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282072'>四明杨子家本三江之口，徙居西屿之麓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282072_comment'></div>绿野横其前，青峦维其外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282072_comment'></div>东海之水，不惮馀百里之劳遥，崎岖委蛇，日致两潮之勤于其门，输清纳润，曾不少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282072_comment'></div>北山之桃李，方春盛时，相与联比，参红错白，间青厕翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282072_comment'></div>组织西蜀之锦，环石鱼之楼而屏之，美于画绘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282072_comment'></div>南园之竹，栉栉差差，如立万琅玕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282072_comment'></div>疏疏剪剪，微风过之，萧然如奏天上之乐于碧云之端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282072_comment'></div>竹之南有水，水之中有荷青圆，有蒲绿纤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282072_comment'></div>水仙微酣而立，炯若出尘之风度，而隔以云烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282072_comment'></div>游鳞戏凉，群群然、圉圉然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282072_comment'></div>至于芙蓉秋红，菊金布钱，橘梢之黄未垂，而葡萄堆架，拥千万夜光之珠而争先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282072_comment'></div>虽朔飙之戒寒，烂丹丘于四山，而压冰之梅独出其奇，吐孤芳而盘旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282072_comment'></div>玄冥又从而佐之，剪玉镂瑶，雨花其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282072_comment'></div>有家如此，亦可谓奇矣，而杨子方悠然而笑曰：吾又有广居焉益奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282072_comment'></div>吾所谓广居，非弃此而他之，特前所陈，有目者之所共瞻，有口者之所共言，吾今所叙，有目者之所不睹，有口者虽欲言而无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282072_comment'></div>广居之上，天所不覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282072_comment'></div>胡为乎天莫之覆也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282072_comment'></div>天可指，天可语，吾之广居不可指，不可语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282072_comment'></div>广居之下，地所不载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282072_comment'></div>胡为乎地莫之载也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282072_comment'></div>地有所起，有所止，吾之广居无所起，无所止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282072_comment'></div>广居之东，其东无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282072_comment'></div>胡为乎无穷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282072_comment'></div>扶桑有名，欲往莫从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282072_comment'></div>阳精朝升，犹在青冥之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282072_comment'></div>青冥有象，有象有穷，无象无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282072_comment'></div>吾广居不可以象言，奚穷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282072_comment'></div>广居之西，其西无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282072_comment'></div>胡为乎无穷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282072_comment'></div>昆崙而西，其远益迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282072_comment'></div>虽极夫日入焉之涯，道阻且脩，已莫之跻，矧其日外之冥冥，与东则齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282072_comment'></div>有涯、有冥冥、有穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282072_comment'></div>无涯、无冥冥，无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1282072_comment'></div>吾广居不可以涯言，不可以冥冥言，奚穷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1282072_comment'></div>广居之南，沧溟渺漫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1282072_comment'></div>海外有国，国外有水，水之外人莫得而观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1282072_comment'></div>可观者必有所穷，吾广居尚不可得而观，奚穷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1282072_comment'></div>广居之北，沙漠无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1282072_comment'></div>骨利干近日出之所，北距大海，海又无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1282072_comment'></div>海虽大，不逃乎形，有形之物终穷，吾广居不可以形，奚穷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1282072_comment'></div>广居之中，天生其中，地生其中，日月经其中，星辰罗其中，雷霆风雨霜雪变化其中，人与鸟兽虫鱼万汇尽产其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1282072_comment'></div>然则所谓杨子者居于其中之何所哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1282072_comment'></div>三江之口乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1282072_comment'></div>西屿之麓乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1282072_comment'></div>室乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1282072_comment'></div>堂乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1282072_comment'></div>序乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1282072_comment'></div>塾乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1282072_comment'></div>石鱼之楼乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1282072_comment'></div>南园之竹坞乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1282072_comment'></div>谓不居乎三江之口不可，谓果居乎三江之口，亦不可；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1282072_comment'></div>谓不徙乎西屿之麓不可，谓果徙乎西屿之麓亦不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1282072_comment'></div>堂无中边，室无户牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1282072_comment'></div>序岂东西，塾非左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1282072_comment'></div>楼虽可登而难升，坞虽可游而莫有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1282072_comment'></div>大哉乎，广居！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1282072_comment'></div>以文宣至圣犹莫知其乡，以洙泗诸侯犹不得其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1282072_comment'></div>学者愈行而愈远，智者愈言而昏者愈不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1282072_comment'></div>壁闼四辟，而宗庙之美、百官之富，非立墙之外者所扪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1282072_comment'></div>是中有不求自有之至乐：宫商日奏，金石日谐，油油而溶溶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1282072_comment'></div>易直子谅，庄敬正中，高明而有融，泰和而粹冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1282072_comment'></div>世乐有穷，斯乐靡终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1282072_comment'></div>举视听心知之属，不以为有旦暮、有古今、有始终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1282072_comment'></div>而寂然莫之移，洞焉乎空空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1282072_comment'></div>缉熙灵府之光明，混涵圣域之冥濛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1282072_comment'></div>而圆首横目之子方且日持钻坚之锥，力运凿深之锄，进寸而退尺，欲前而倒趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1282072_comment'></div>嘻嘻，吁吁！</div><div id='poem_sentence_66_1282072_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　撰《南园赋》，姑系于本年。<div id='poem_1282073' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282073' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282073?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南园赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282073")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282073_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282073'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282073'>光风兮静明，林塘兮翠深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282073_comment'></div>云闲兮不动，景妙兮莫寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282073_comment'></div>泰和融凝兮非浮而非沈，万化迭奏兮岂去曩而来今？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282073_comment'></div>不知吾足之所如往兮，不觉吾口之自吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282073_comment'></div>百草千木兮，散苍然之球琳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282073_comment'></div>纷禽鸟之飞鸣兮，尽成韶頀之音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282073_comment'></div>乐悠悠以自生兮，孰究其所始、究其所终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282073_comment'></div>微觉其略如万象兮，森罗杂错于止水之上、明鉴之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282073_comment'></div>纤洪短脩毕陈互映兮，有不可胜穷之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282073_comment'></div>而澄光莹然兮，曾莫省其聚散，矧复判其西东？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282073_comment'></div>厥沈兮匪卑，厥高兮岂穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282073_comment'></div>其骤焉辐辏兮非积，其忽焉以遁遂至于无兮讵空？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282073_comment'></div>斯妙兮可言而不可语，惟可弄明月兮歌清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282073_comment'></div>不索自获兮愈思愈穷，古之人何以命之曰中庸？</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1282073_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　撰《蛙乐赋》，姑系于本年。<div id='poem_1282075' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282075' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282075?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蛙乐赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282075")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282075_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282075'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282075'>至矣乎，至矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282075_comment'></div>音声之妙，有如此不可以言道，不可以意传者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282075_comment'></div>静夜兮寂然，发机兮捷然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282075_comment'></div>有唱辄酬兮，翕然骤然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282075_comment'></div>千鼗竞奏，万珠纷联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282075_comment'></div>此断兮彼续，甲洪兮乙纤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282075_comment'></div>各出其奇，互发其妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282075_comment'></div>离离然，粲粲然，若星辰之缀悬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282075_comment'></div>泠泠然，激激然，若岩隈之溜，涧下之泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282075_comment'></div>又若急雨过潇湘之上，织锦濯蜀江之芳鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282075_comment'></div>宫商迭播，角羽相先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282075_comment'></div>律不知其何律兮，吕不知其何吕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282075_comment'></div>惟睹夫大积焉而不苑，并行而不谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282075_comment'></div>随之不见其后，迎之不见其前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282075_comment'></div>如彼万象森罗，参错毕见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282075_comment'></div>其莹然之鉴，澄然之渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282075_comment'></div>至动矣而静，至繁矣而不喧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282075_comment'></div>是音也可闻而不可听，可以默识而不可口宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282075_comment'></div>孔圣遇之而忘齐国之肉味，黄帝得之而大张于洞庭之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282075_comment'></div>胡为乎独不见省于横目之士，至憎而为烦？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282075_comment'></div>甚以为冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282075_comment'></div>冤矣乎，冤矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282075_comment'></div>俯不睹其为地，仰莫知其为天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282075_comment'></div>虽百师旷何所措其耳，虽千子期恶从探其源？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282075_comment'></div>然则是其要妙终而不出其秘，以启后来之惓惓者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282075_comment'></div>西屿杨子于是为之歌曰：竹风之萧然，松月之炯然，佐以丝桐之洒然，继以是歌之油油然，可谓昭然灼然。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1282075_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　撰《月赋》，姑系于本年。<div id='poem_1282076' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282076' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282076?labeling=true' target='_blank'>月赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282076")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282076_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282076'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282076'>山月兮腾腾，千峰兮毕明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282076_comment'></div>入林度岭兮，疏爽而散清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282076_comment'></div>浮波泛流兮，又何其萦回潋滟，湛湛渟渟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282076_comment'></div>云气尽伏，太虚碧澄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282076_comment'></div>不疾而速，不行而至，忽一轮之骤升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282076_comment'></div>珠无得以肖其圆，玉不可以齐其莹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282076_comment'></div>神光独奇，万古一灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282076_comment'></div>遁星辰之失色，截天汉之欲倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282076_comment'></div>虚明之妙，弥满六合，拟揽之而无得，姑触之而莫○。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282076_comment'></div>入竹则与之为竹，入松则与之为松，到几盈几，透窗满棂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282076_comment'></div>彻酒涵杯，跨弦诣琴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282076_comment'></div>大巧造微至于此而无所用其力，至洁非染而如留若凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282076_comment'></div>却之似止而非止，进之似临而非临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282076_comment'></div>自古幽人雅士，孰不仰止玩止，乐之咏之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282076_comment'></div>不知其几千万语矣，终莫能赞其不可摹写之奇，探其造化机缄之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282076_comment'></div>广寒宫殿近在吾方寸之地，而有目者无睹，有耳者未聆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282076_comment'></div>西屿杨子，女知之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282076_comment'></div>杨子曰：「子惟无知，故若是乐也，故若是融融皓皓，迎之不见其首，随之不见其后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282076_comment'></div>且不自知其为无知，而况于知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282076_comment'></div>子仰而观之，清明者何乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282076_comment'></div>俯而履之，博厚者何乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282076_comment'></div>从子目之所视，所视者何乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282076_comment'></div>从子耳之所闻，所闻者何乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282076_comment'></div>彼乎，此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282076_comment'></div>巨乎，细乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282076_comment'></div>虚乎，实乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282076_comment'></div>众乎，寡乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282076_comment'></div>有乎，无乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282076_comment'></div>子乎，我乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282076_comment'></div>可言乎，不可言乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282076_comment'></div>可思乎，不可思乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282076_comment'></div>洙泗圣人所以无得而称，姑托之以水，曰知者乐之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282076_comment'></div>又托之以山，曰仁者乐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1282076_comment'></div>某今亦姑赋之以月，而某乐乐之，子信乎」？</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1282076_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　撰《心画赋》，姑系于本年。<div id='poem_1282077' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282077' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282077?labeling=true' target='_blank'>心画赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282077")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282077_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282077'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282077'>砚者，天池也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282077_comment'></div>墨者，玄云也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282077_comment'></div>笔者，龙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282077_comment'></div>乘龙者，不知其为何神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282077_comment'></div>迎之不见其首，随之不见其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282077_comment'></div>操则存，舍则亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282077_comment'></div>出入无时，莫知其乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282077_comment'></div>忽焉有感而动，乘龙饮天池之水，运磨玄云，须臾下膏泽以润洽万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282077_comment'></div>随物为形，为圆为方，为正为旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282077_comment'></div>或直而遂，或曲而彊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282077_comment'></div>或来或往，如飞如翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282077_comment'></div>如金如玉，如斋如庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282077_comment'></div>变化万状，众善中藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282077_comment'></div>粹然之容，烨然之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282077_comment'></div>其不可穷尽之妙，岂钟、王、欧、虞诸子所能梦而见、觉而望？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282077_comment'></div>彼方且驰骛矜衒乎放荡之晋世，以文饰奸，可耻可叹之唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282077_comment'></div>后世又从而祖述之，不复知三代之王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282077_comment'></div>古列圣人典章钟鼎刻画具在，睹之使人温良恭敬，中正精粹之德生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282077_comment'></div>今观《兰亭》遗稿，亦有油然感动于中者乎亡？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282077_comment'></div>吁吁嘻嘻！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282077_comment'></div>坏人心，败风俗，使成人鲜德，小子无造，享国者不长，皆斯类有以共成其殃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282077_comment'></div>而天下犹不知其故，反相与助其狂澜，撷其馀芳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1282077_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　遣奠吕子约，姑系于本年。作品：《奠辞》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明文章名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年4月</a>　取曾子之书，参古本而厘正之，释其疑义。四月序。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年9月9日</a>　此日，邑人求撰《春秋祀董孝君辞》，姑系于此。<div id='poem_1282267' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282267' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282267?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邑人求春秋祀董孝君词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1197年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282267")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282267_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282267'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282267'>夫孝，人心之所同，天地之所同，鬼神之所同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282267_comment'></div>徵君用此心于千载之上，吾邑人敬而奉之于千载之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282267_comment'></div>岂惟邑人敬而奉之，一郡之人敬而奉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282267_comment'></div>岂惟一郡之人敬而奉之，际天所覆，凡在人伦中者有所不知，知则孰不敬而奉之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282267_comment'></div>呜呼至矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282267_comment'></div>是谓至德，是谓要道，是谓人心之所同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282267_comment'></div>惟尔有神惠相之，俾某暨兹在位，永保所自有之本心，以对越明神，以对越上帝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1282267_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年2月16日</a>　此日，会从妗臧孺人卢氏葬于鄞县桃源乡西山万隩。志从舅翰林医痊臧宾卿墓。作品：《翰林臧公墓铭》<div id='poem_1282222' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282222' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282222?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋翰林医痊臧公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆元四年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1198年2月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282222")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282222_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282222'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282222'>某之外曾王父臧公讳中立，本毗陵之无锡人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282222_comment'></div>为儒，而通于黄帝、岐伯之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282222_comment'></div>乐四明山水而徙焉，今六世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282222_comment'></div>娶无锡承氏，生五男子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282222_comment'></div>长讳师心，次讳师旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282222_comment'></div>次讳师颜，是为翰林医候，累赠从义郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282222_comment'></div>次讳师文，是为某之外王父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282222_comment'></div>以文行升上舍，贡礼部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282222_comment'></div>次讳师皋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282222_comment'></div>某自识事，已不及见外王父母矣，惟省总角侍母孺人归外氏，犹及见外伯祖母从义孺人倪氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282222_comment'></div>诸舅环侍，朱紫满前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282222_comment'></div>今妣舅俱亡，而诸妗又亡，伤今念昔，哀动于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282222_comment'></div>比会从妗孺人卢氏葬，从表兄属某志铭从舅医痊墓，并叙二妗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282222_comment'></div>某属卑德下，惧莫之任，表兄勉谕于再于三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282222_comment'></div>某不得而逊，乃退考其行实，已而叹曰：正道之不明于天下也，盖自周衰，以迄五代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282222_comment'></div>周六官分职，皆所以为民极，极者天下极致之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282222_comment'></div>而天官之属有医师焉，有疾医焉，盖上士、中士为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282222_comment'></div>古之为士，异乎后之为士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282222_comment'></div>古之士以德行道艺，后之士大抵以文辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282222_comment'></div>是故品流之论兴，而是非之实殽乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282222_comment'></div>夫天下极致之道，惟其是而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282222_comment'></div>舍天下公是公非而虚文而侈，是无惑乎后世之风俗日趋于敝，而不反古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282222_comment'></div>皇宋举三代之遗制，建百官，一道德，而习俗之固犹滞于流品之论，岂其人犹或未有公是之实耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282222_comment'></div>若吾外氏则有公是之实矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282222_comment'></div>从义之戒子曰：「疾者之求于我，当怀恻隐，毋以利为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282222_comment'></div>违吾言，为不孝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282222_comment'></div>医痊讳宾卿，字云叟，从义之仲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282222_comment'></div>亦急于救物，不以贫富贵贱二其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282222_comment'></div>医有能而无资，公推挽，俾尽所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282222_comment'></div>药必己给，报必彼归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282222_comment'></div>其不啬不忘如此，是非公是之实耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282222_comment'></div>善无大小，道无精粗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282222_comment'></div>公和而不同，不妄言笑，遇事若无所可否；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1282222_comment'></div>至大义所在，则介于石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1282222_comment'></div>公以谨厚闻于乡，郡太守多所爱重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1282222_comment'></div>有故旧罹横逆，公悯其无辜，思为一言，其家忽盛金帛以请，公正色却之，曰：「女以物豢我，吾不复为言矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1282222_comment'></div>其妻与子罗拜泣曰：「今不敢以累清德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1282222_comment'></div>卒白其冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1282222_comment'></div>后踵门来谢，亦不之纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1282222_comment'></div>斯固士君子常行，而文辞之士间有不能，是又非公是之实耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1282222_comment'></div>公孝友儒雅，闺门雍穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1282222_comment'></div>初以侍从参奏试翰林院，补翰林医学，累转至医痊，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1282222_comment'></div>隆兴元年六月八日卒，寿五十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1282222_comment'></div>明年十有一月丙申葬于鄞县桃源乡之西山万岙，合先室卢氏之藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1282222_comment'></div>卢氏顺事舅姑，睦于姒娣，内外无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1282222_comment'></div>绍兴十有一年十有一月二十有九日卒，寿三十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1282222_comment'></div>丙寅九月乙酉乃克葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1282222_comment'></div>戊寅郊赉赠孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1282222_comment'></div>医痊再娶卢氏女弟，亦封孺人，后赐冠帔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1282222_comment'></div>孝谨之行，如其女兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1282222_comment'></div>壮年孀居，遂弃铅华，终身德性澹然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1282222_comment'></div>人奉之不喜，忤之不怒，是非荣辱不以动其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1282222_comment'></div>时时诵「却除蔽惑滋成疾，趣向高明又是邪」之句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1282222_comment'></div>一日梦神人告之曰：「女寿五十二，今以积德延七十六」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1282222_comment'></div>及属纩之夕，安然如寐，实庆元三年十有一月二十有五日，寿七十六，符神人所告云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1282222_comment'></div>明年十月甲申，合葬于万岙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1282222_comment'></div>子男三，皆儒学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1282222_comment'></div>长讳泳，绍兴元年四月二十有三日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1282222_comment'></div>次讳济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1282222_comment'></div>季讳沔，淳熙十有五年七月十有二日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1282222_comment'></div>女二：长适承直郎、□州学教授卢子即，从妗之从侄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1282222_comment'></div>次适里士陆檍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1282222_comment'></div>孙男十有三人：植登绍兴四年进士科，迪功郎、常州晋陵县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1282222_comment'></div>格登庆元五年进士科，迪功郎、新绍兴府诸暨县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1282222_comment'></div>杞、楷、枱、松、棫、枃、楠、栻、枋、枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1282222_comment'></div>孙女五：长适赣教授子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1282222_comment'></div>次适玉牒承信郎□通夫，次适太学生史弥巩，次适里士舒涛，次适里士章德甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1282222_comment'></div>曾孙男十有七：元善、元谨、元吉、元庆，馀未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1282222_comment'></div>女十有五，俱未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1282222_comment'></div>不胜含哀起敬，而铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_1282222'>皇极之敷言，是彝是训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1282222_comment'></div>道一以贯，孰精而深，孰肤而近？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1282222_comment'></div>胡不闻先圣之言曰，「中庸之为德，其至矣乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1282222_comment'></div>庸，常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1282222_comment'></div>猗与舅妗，德性正顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1282222_comment'></div>有皇极焉，人毋易之，自起遁离之病。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1282222_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='394c27ea4fa04831ab730973f19044f7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("394c27ea4fa04831ab730973f19044f7");'><span id='394c27ea4fa04831ab730973f19044f7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1208')">1199-1208年</a>，59-68岁</div><div id='394c27ea4fa04831ab730973f19044f7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年12月15日</a>　此日，志舒元质墓。作品：《志》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明志文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1200&endYear=1200')">1200年</a>　主管崇道观，再任朝奉郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1201&endYear=1201')">1201年</a>　此日，有所悟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1202&endYear=1202')">1202年</a>　祖奠冯氏姊。作品：《奠辞》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明文章名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1203&endYear=1203')">1203年</a>　嘉泰昭阳大渊献，筑室董孝君祠之西，下有湖焉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1203&endYear=1203')">1203年</a>　撰《先圣大训》<div id='poem_1282118' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282118' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282118?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先圣大训序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1203年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282118")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282118_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282118'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282118'>世称先圣，谓孔子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282118_comment'></div>某祗惟先圣大训自《论语》、《孝经》、《易》、《春秋》而外，散落隐伏，虽间见于杂说之中，而不尊不特，有讹有诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282118_comment'></div>道心大同，昏明斯异，毫釐有间，虽面觌无睹，明告莫谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282118_comment'></div>是无惑乎圣言则一，而记者不同也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282118_comment'></div>又无惑乎承舛听谬，遂至于大乖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282118_comment'></div>夜光之珠，久混沙砾，日月之明，出没云气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282118_comment'></div>不知固无责，有知焉而不致其力，非义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282118_comment'></div>是用参證群记，聚而为一书，刊诬阙疑，发幽出隐，庶乎不至滋后学之惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282118_comment'></div>非敢以是为确也，敬俟哲人审订胥正。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1282118_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年1月</a>　是月，撰《安康太夫人奠辞》<div id='poem_1282256' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282256' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282256?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奠安康郡太夫人辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1204年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282256")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282256_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282256'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282256'>具位杨某谨奉奠于故安康郡太夫人祖筵曰：于乎哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282256_comment'></div>道无不明，人自不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282256_comment'></div>天地之道，为物不二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282256_comment'></div>人天地心，三才一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282256_comment'></div>自学子裂坤道于乾元之外，置天地于人心之外，而先圣之道始不明于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282256_comment'></div>虽古烈妇贤母载在简策，人所知敬，而道终未明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282256_comment'></div>于乎哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282256_comment'></div>夫人淑德懿行，某夙昔而不得备知，而辱在州里，又辱知于尚书，因尚书而获修登堂再拜之敬，望见揄翟之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282256_comment'></div>退而得诸亲知，夫人博观古书，中秉正德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282256_comment'></div>居既富且贵人所不敢仰望之地，而至朴至俭，服有人所不堪之衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282256_comment'></div>某闻不胜起敬起慕，曰：夫人之贤行如此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282256_comment'></div>又尚书尝道其燕侍之言，确乎不动于势利，清哉，伟哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282256_comment'></div>今又获尚书所状行实，启读熟复，益视其所未知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282256_comment'></div>母仪坤德，某灼知其为天地不贰之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282256_comment'></div>往往蚩蚩横目，未必咸知，就知之不能无疑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282256_comment'></div>而某确信之，断断乎无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282256_comment'></div>胡不考诸《易》乎，「日用而不知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282256_comment'></div>夫惟不自知，是以人虽有道，亦莫之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282256_comment'></div>有奠在筵，有铭在旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282256_comment'></div>商祝读辞，道由是明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282256_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1282256_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年春</a>　春，记昌国州申义堂。作品：《记》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明记文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年</a>　沈文彪以奥学峻行与杨文元为忘年交，尝别筑亭馆招文元讲道其中，命子民献、婿刘厚南执经座下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年</a>　有诗。作品：《登石鱼楼诗三首》<div id='poem_131305' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131305' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131305?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登石鱼楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1204年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_131305")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_131305_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131305'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131305'>楼栏倚碧空，绿树正摇风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131305'>我独来从容，笑歌于其中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131305'>微凉吹我衣，碧袂纱玲珑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131305'>诗成自长吟，宛转音和融。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131305'>此意无人会，祇许清风同。<div id='poem_sentence_4_131305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_131305'>亦许空间云，悠然西又东。<div id='poem_sentence_5_131305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_131305'>亦许林间禽，幽啭声无踪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_131305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_131305'>亦许山间翁，笑语天机通。<div id='poem_sentence_7_131305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_131305'>前山对我吟，突兀青重重。<div id='poem_sentence_8_131305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_131305'>终日赓我歌，知音无瞽宗。<div id='poem_sentence_9_131305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_131305'>知音自古少，日月空临照。<div id='poem_sentence_10_131305_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_131305'>天地终不秘，造化今未了。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年</a>　有著作，姑系于本年。作品：《石鱼偶记》<div id='poem_207359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_207359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/207359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>偶成<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作曹彦约诗）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1204年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_207359")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div
