href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年</a>　有《焚黄祝文》<div id='poem_1282298' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282298' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282298?labeling=true' target='_blank'>焚黄祝文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1204年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282298")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282298_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282298'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282298'>孝子某敢告考君赠朝散郎、妣君赠安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282298_comment'></div>既告于庙，更题神主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282298_comment'></div>兹焫告黄，谨以嘉蔬清酌庶羞祗荐墓几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282298_comment'></div>钦惟先德，肇本天贶，答之滋至未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282298_comment'></div>某敢不兢兢恪修，率迪丕训，庶无坠遗绪？</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1282298_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年</a>　奠冯氏妹。作品：《奠辞》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明文章名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年</a>　简年六十四，始省偏与党相近而微不同。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1205&endYear=1205')">1205年6月29日</a>　此日，序《象山集》作品：《序》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明序文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年</a>　撰《祖奠姪妇舒氏》<div id='poem_1282260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祖奠侄妇舒氏辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282260")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282260'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282260'>叔舅某兹祭奠于亡侄妇舒氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282260_comment'></div>就封有期，酌酒以告妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282260_comment'></div>吾友西美之子来相侄怿，旦旦登堂叙揖，时节叙拜，祀事相礼，凡百惟肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282260_comment'></div>近怿有觉，转以告妇，乃克领会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282260_comment'></div>且曰：「特以分严，有愿陈于叔舅之前，当益有启明之意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282260_comment'></div>疾革，又觉截不殿屎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282260_comment'></div>于乎哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282260_comment'></div>于乎善哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282260_comment'></div>怿复告某，妇秉礼严，默符先圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282260_comment'></div>于乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282260_comment'></div>侄妇有至德善行如此，叔舅未之知，乃今知之，而遂隔幽明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282260_comment'></div>于乎哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282260_comment'></div>叔舅朽质，新年六十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282260_comment'></div>不可冒寒风，酌奠以别，辞噎莫继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282260_comment'></div>哀哉哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282260_comment'></div>哀哉哀哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1282260_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年12月14日</a>　孙应时葬于十二月十四日，为撰墓志铭。作品：《孙季和圹志》<div id='poem_1282227' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282227' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282227?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙烛武先生圹志<span class='inlineComment2'>（开禧二年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年12月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282227")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282227_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282227'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282227'>孙烛武先生应时，越之馀姚人也，今为绍兴府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282227_comment'></div>曾祖讳政，祖讳子全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282227_comment'></div>父讳介，累封赠承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282227_comment'></div>某与季和承学于江西象山陆先生，季和由是信此心本善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282227_comment'></div>方相与讲切进德，而开禧二年二月甲戌不禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282227_comment'></div>季和早入太学，淳熙乙未登进士第，为台州黄岩尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282227_comment'></div>士民爱之，欲其置田宅留居焉，辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282227_comment'></div>后丞泰州海陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282227_comment'></div>丁承议君忧，服阕，为严州遂安令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282227_comment'></div>从蜀帅邱公崇之辟，邑人不得而留，至于哭送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282227_comment'></div>大将有世袭，朝廷患之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282227_comment'></div>邱公因其病，使季和往视疾，以察军情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282227_comment'></div>盛礼十献，辞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282227_comment'></div>复命，以事告邱公，遂奏易他姓，厥功茂矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282227_comment'></div>改秩知平江府常熟县，垂满，太守以仓粟累政流欠三千斛见问，士民陈词，愿共偿，不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282227_comment'></div>竟闻于朝，贬秩罢归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282227_comment'></div>后授通判邵武军，将赴而已病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282227_comment'></div>历官至承议郎，后以致仕转朝奉郎，寿五十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282227_comment'></div>冬十有二月庚申葬于县之龙泉乡竹山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282227_comment'></div>娶张氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282227_comment'></div>子祖开，方九龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282227_comment'></div>三女：长适文正范公五世孙克家，次适宣义郎义乌丞胡衍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282227_comment'></div>葬日薄，嘉言善行不备书，姑识其略于圹石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282227_comment'></div>朝散郎、主管建昌军杨简书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1282227_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年</a>　读《大禹谟》，有所省。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年</a>　代冯似宗撰《寿楼文昌》诗。<div id='poem_472865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_472865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/472865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代冯似宗寿楼文昌<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_472865")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_472865_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_472865_0'>① 维公寿宫使阁学尚书楼公也表弟冯某作是诗再拜以献焉</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_472865'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_472865'>维山四明，涵奇孕英。<div id='poem_sentence_0_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_472865'>或曰降神，为今甫申。<div id='poem_sentence_1_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_472865'>倬彼云汉，昭回其文。<div id='poem_sentence_2_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_472865'>凤鸣朝阳，决河昆崙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_472865'>代天而言，粹其德音。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_4_472865_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_472865'>补衮大手，石色五有。<div id='poem_sentence_5_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_472865'>砥柱中流，屹屹其守。<div id='poem_sentence_6_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_472865'>为人所难，一辞万口。<div id='poem_sentence_7_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_472865'>文昌大名，太山北斗。<span class='charType'>（二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_8_472865_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_472865'>云归星驾，持麾东下。<div id='poem_sentence_9_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_472865'>乘流御风，琳宫燕暇。<div id='poem_sentence_10_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_472865'>山水清晖，亲戚情话。<div id='poem_sentence_11_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_472865'>不间遐贱，如某某者。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_12_472865_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_472865'>肆筵设席，获教蒙益。<div id='poem_sentence_13_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_472865'>缱绻绸缪，问遗不息。<div id='poem_sentence_14_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_472865'>万金良药，再生大德。<span class='charType'>（四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_15_472865_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_472865'>阳复之望，惟公诞辰。<div id='poem_sentence_16_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_472865'>何以贶之，秉国之钧。<div id='poem_sentence_17_472865_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_472865'>何以寿之，南山之椿。<span class='charType'>（五章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_18_472865_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_472865'></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_472865_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1207&endYear=1207')">1207年3月21日</a>　林硕葬于此日，为撰墓志铭。作品：《林硕墓志铭》<div id='poem_1282222' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282222' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282222?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋翰林医痊臧公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆元四年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1198年2月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282222")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282222_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282222'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282222'>某之外曾王父臧公讳中立，本毗陵之无锡人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282222_comment'></div>为儒，而通于黄帝、岐伯之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282222_comment'></div>乐四明山水而徙焉，今六世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282222_comment'></div>娶无锡承氏，生五男子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282222_comment'></div>长讳师心，次讳师旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282222_comment'></div>次讳师颜，是为翰林医候，累赠从义郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282222_comment'></div>次讳师文，是为某之外王父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282222_comment'></div>以文行升上舍，贡礼部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282222_comment'></div>次讳师皋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282222_comment'></div>某自识事，已不及见外王父母矣，惟省总角侍母孺人归外氏，犹及见外伯祖母从义孺人倪氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282222_comment'></div>诸舅环侍，朱紫满前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282222_comment'></div>今妣舅俱亡，而诸妗又亡，伤今念昔，哀动于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282222_comment'></div>比会从妗孺人卢氏葬，从表兄属某志铭从舅医痊墓，并叙二妗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282222_comment'></div>某属卑德下，惧莫之任，表兄勉谕于再于三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282222_comment'></div>某不得而逊，乃退考其行实，已而叹曰：正道之不明于天下也，盖自周衰，以迄五代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282222_comment'></div>周六官分职，皆所以为民极，极者天下极致之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282222_comment'></div>而天官之属有医师焉，有疾医焉，盖上士、中士为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282222_comment'></div>古之为士，异乎后之为士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282222_comment'></div>古之士以德行道艺，后之士大抵以文辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282222_comment'></div>是故品流之论兴，而是非之实殽乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282222_comment'></div>夫天下极致之道，惟其是而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282222_comment'></div>舍天下公是公非而虚文而侈，是无惑乎后世之风俗日趋于敝，而不反古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282222_comment'></div>皇宋举三代之遗制，建百官，一道德，而习俗之固犹滞于流品之论，岂其人犹或未有公是之实耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282222_comment'></div>若吾外氏则有公是之实矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282222_comment'></div>从义之戒子曰：「疾者之求于我，当怀恻隐，毋以利为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282222_comment'></div>违吾言，为不孝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282222_comment'></div>医痊讳宾卿，字云叟，从义之仲子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282222_comment'></div>亦急于救物，不以贫富贵贱二其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282222_comment'></div>医有能而无资，公推挽，俾尽所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282222_comment'></div>药必己给，报必彼归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282222_comment'></div>其不啬不忘如此，是非公是之实耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282222_comment'></div>善无大小，道无精粗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282222_comment'></div>公和而不同，不妄言笑，遇事若无所可否；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1282222_comment'></div>至大义所在，则介于石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1282222_comment'></div>公以谨厚闻于乡，郡太守多所爱重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1282222_comment'></div>有故旧罹横逆，公悯其无辜，思为一言，其家忽盛金帛以请，公正色却之，曰：「女以物豢我，吾不复为言矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1282222_comment'></div>其妻与子罗拜泣曰：「今不敢以累清德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1282222_comment'></div>卒白其冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1282222_comment'></div>后踵门来谢，亦不之纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1282222_comment'></div>斯固士君子常行，而文辞之士间有不能，是又非公是之实耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1282222_comment'></div>公孝友儒雅，闺门雍穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1282222_comment'></div>初以侍从参奏试翰林院，补翰林医学，累转至医痊，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1282222_comment'></div>隆兴元年六月八日卒，寿五十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1282222_comment'></div>明年十有一月丙申葬于鄞县桃源乡之西山万岙，合先室卢氏之藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1282222_comment'></div>卢氏顺事舅姑，睦于姒娣，内外无间言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1282222_comment'></div>绍兴十有一年十有一月二十有九日卒，寿三十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1282222_comment'></div>丙寅九月乙酉乃克葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1282222_comment'></div>戊寅郊赉赠孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1282222_comment'></div>医痊再娶卢氏女弟，亦封孺人，后赐冠帔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1282222_comment'></div>孝谨之行，如其女兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1282222_comment'></div>壮年孀居，遂弃铅华，终身德性澹然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1282222_comment'></div>人奉之不喜，忤之不怒，是非荣辱不以动其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1282222_comment'></div>时时诵「却除蔽惑滋成疾，趣向高明又是邪」之句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1282222_comment'></div>一日梦神人告之曰：「女寿五十二，今以积德延七十六」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1282222_comment'></div>及属纩之夕，安然如寐，实庆元三年十有一月二十有五日，寿七十六，符神人所告云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1282222_comment'></div>明年十月甲申，合葬于万岙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1282222_comment'></div>子男三，皆儒学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1282222_comment'></div>长讳泳，绍兴元年四月二十有三日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1282222_comment'></div>次讳济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1282222_comment'></div>季讳沔，淳熙十有五年七月十有二日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1282222_comment'></div>女二：长适承直郎、□州学教授卢子即，从妗之从侄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1282222_comment'></div>次适里士陆檍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1282222_comment'></div>孙男十有三人：植登绍兴四年进士科，迪功郎、常州晋陵县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1282222_comment'></div>格登庆元五年进士科，迪功郎、新绍兴府诸暨县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1282222_comment'></div>杞、楷、枱、松、棫、枃、楠、栻、枋、枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1282222_comment'></div>孙女五：长适赣教授子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1282222_comment'></div>次适玉牒承信郎□通夫，次适太学生史弥巩，次适里士舒涛，次适里士章德甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1282222_comment'></div>曾孙男十有七：元善、元谨、元吉、元庆，馀未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1282222_comment'></div>女十有五，俱未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1282222_comment'></div>不胜含哀起敬，而铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_1282222'>皇极之敷言，是彝是训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1282222_comment'></div>道一以贯，孰精而深，孰肤而近？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1282222_comment'></div>胡不闻先圣之言曰，「中庸之为德，其至矣乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1282222_comment'></div>庸，常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1282222_comment'></div>猗与舅妗，德性正顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1282222_comment'></div>有皇极焉，人毋易之，自起遁离之病。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1282222_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1207&endYear=1207')">1207年3月27日</a>　孙之翰葬于此日，为撰墓志铭。作品：《志》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明志文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1207&endYear=1207')">1207年</a>　与叶秀发、詹阜民、顾平甫交，姑系于本年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1208&endYear=1208')">1208年</a>　门人曾熠刊《己易》、《孔子闲居解》。六月六日，赵彦悈书后。十月六日，又书。十一月，曾熠书后。<div id='poem_1282163' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282163' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282163?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孔子閒居解</a><span class='authorDate'>（1208年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282163")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282163_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282163'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282163'>孔子閒居，子夏侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282163_comment'></div>子夏曰：「敢问《诗》云『凯弟君子，民之父母』，何如斯可谓民之父母矣」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282163_comment'></div>孔子曰：「夫民之父母乎，必达于礼乐之原，以致<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>五至</span>，而行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>三无</span>，以横于天下，四方有败必先知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282163_comment'></div>此之谓民之父母矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282163_comment'></div>子夏曰：「民之父母，既得而闻之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282163_comment'></div>敢问何谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/17/Comments/1")'>五至</span>」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282163_comment'></div>孔子曰：「志之所至，诗亦至焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282163_comment'></div>诗之所至，礼亦至焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282163_comment'></div>礼之所至，乐亦至焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282163_comment'></div>乐之所至，哀亦至焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282163_comment'></div>哀乐相生，是故正明目而视之，不可得而见也，倾耳而听之，不可得而闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282163_comment'></div>志气塞乎天地，此之谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/33/Comments/1")'>五至</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282163_comment'></div>子夏曰：「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/35/Comments/1")'>五至</span>既得而闻之矣，敢问何谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/36/Comments/1")'>三无</span>」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282163_comment'></div>孔子曰：「无声之乐，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>，此之谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/41/Comments/1")'>三无</span>」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282163_comment'></div>子夏曰：「<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/43/Comments/1")'>三无</span>既得略而闻之矣，敢问何诗近之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282163_comment'></div>孔子曰：「『夙夜基命宥密』，无声之乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282163_comment'></div>『威仪逮逮，不可选也』，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282163_comment'></div>『凡民有丧，匍匐救之』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/53/Comments/1")'>无服之丧</span>也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282163_comment'></div>子夏曰：「言则大矣，美矣，盛矣，言尽于此而已乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282163_comment'></div>孔子曰：「何为其然也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282163_comment'></div>君子之服之也，犹有五起焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282163_comment'></div>子夏曰：「何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282163_comment'></div>孔子曰：「无声之乐，气志不违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，威仪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>迟迟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>，内恕孔悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282163_comment'></div>无声之乐，气志既得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/74/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，威仪翼翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>，施及四国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282163_comment'></div>无声之乐，气志既从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/80/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，上下和同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>，以畜万邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282163_comment'></div>无声之乐，日闻四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/86/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，日就月将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/88/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>，纯德孔明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1282163_comment'></div>无声之乐，气志既起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，施及四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/94/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>，施于孙子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1282163_comment'></div>子夏曰：「三王之德，参于天地，敢问何如斯可谓参天地矣」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1282163_comment'></div>孔子曰：「奉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/101/Comments/1")'>三无</span>私，以劳天下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1282163_comment'></div>子夏曰：「敢问何谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/104/Comments/2")'>三无</span>私」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1282163_comment'></div>孔子曰：「天无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/106/Comments/1")'>私覆</span>，地无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/107/Comments/0")'>私载</span>，日月无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>私照</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1282163_comment'></div>奉斯三者，以劳天下，此之谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/111/Comments/0")'>三无</span>私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1282163_comment'></div>其在诗曰：『帝命不违，至于汤齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1282163_comment'></div>汤降不迟，圣敬日齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1282163_comment'></div>昭假<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/117/Comments/0")'>迟迟</span>，上帝是祗，帝命式于九围』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1282163_comment'></div>是汤之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1282163_comment'></div>天有四时，春秋冬夏，风雨霜露，无非教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1282163_comment'></div>地载神气，神气风霆，风霆流形，庶物露生，无非教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1282163_comment'></div>清明在躬，气志如神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1282163_comment'></div>嗜欲将至，有开必先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1282163_comment'></div>天降时雨，山川出云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1282163_comment'></div>其在《诗》曰：『嵩高维岳，骏极于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1282163_comment'></div>维岳降神，生甫及申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1282163_comment'></div>维申及甫，维周之翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1282163_comment'></div>四国于蕃，四方于宣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1282163_comment'></div>此文武之德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1282163_comment'></div>三代之王也，必先其令闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1282163_comment'></div>诗云『明明天子，令闻不已』，三代之德也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1282163_comment'></div>『弛其文德，协此四国』，大王之德也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1282163_comment'></div>子夏蹶然而起，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/155/Comments/0")'>负墙</span>而立，曰：「弟子敢不承乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1282163_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_1282163'>礼乐之原即<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/158/Comments/0")'>五至</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/159/Comments/0")'>五至</span>即<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/159/Comments/1")'>三无</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/160/Comments/0")'>三无</span>即五起，五起即能先知四方之败者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1282163_comment'></div>道不可言，孔子欲无言，不得已而有言，曰「原」足矣，何必言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/166/Comments/0")'>五至</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/167/Comments/0")'>五至</span>多矣，又何必言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_63_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/168/Comments/0")'>三无</span>？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1282163_comment'></div>子夏沈溺于文义之渊薮，断非一语之所能晓，敷而明之，曲而畅之，庶几或触其机也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1282163_comment'></div>何谓至？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1282163_comment'></div>人皆有心志，即志即至，无所复至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1282163_comment'></div>凡志之有所思焉，有所感焉，思亦何所思，感亦何所感？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1282163_comment'></div>思无所思，人自以为思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1282163_comment'></div>感无所感，人自以为感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1282163_comment'></div>倏然而思，思无所起；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1282163_comment'></div>思而又思，思无所止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1282163_comment'></div>人自以为止，所止者何所？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1282163_comment'></div>厥思亦何物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1282163_comment'></div>执之而无得，视之而无睹，莫究厥始，莫穷厥终，莫执厥中，是之谓大同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1282163_comment'></div>倏然而感，感无所起；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1282163_comment'></div>感而又感，感无所止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1282163_comment'></div>人自以为止，所止者何所？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1282163_comment'></div>厥感亦何物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1282163_comment'></div>执之而无得，视之而无睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1282163_comment'></div>或曰气，气亦中无有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1282163_comment'></div>或曰心，心亦无本体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1282163_comment'></div>莫究厥始，莫穷厥终，莫执厥中，是之谓大同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1282163_comment'></div>若然，则由志而为诗，诗亦然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1282163_comment'></div>发于礼仪，礼亦然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1282163_comment'></div>于是乎乐生，不知手之舞之，足之蹈之，则乐亦然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1282163_comment'></div>人情亦岂能终月乐，终年乐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1282163_comment'></div>亦有哀焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1282163_comment'></div>有所恻焉则哀，有所伤焉则哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1282163_comment'></div>或哀焉，或乐焉，哀乐相生，其变万状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1282163_comment'></div>于戏，至哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1282163_comment'></div>孔子曰，此虽使正明目而视之，不可得而见也，倾耳而听之，不可得而闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1282163_comment'></div>哀虽至于哭颜渊，恸矣，而不自知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1282163_comment'></div>乐虽至于孟子喜而不寐，亦不可见，不可闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1282163_comment'></div>哀乐必有物，非不可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1282163_comment'></div>哭笑必有声，非不可闻也，而圣人断然曰「不可见，不可闻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1282163_comment'></div>众人之乐皆不可见，不可闻也，而众人自以为可见可闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1282163_comment'></div>众人之哀皆不可见，不可闻也，而众人自以为可见可闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1282163_comment'></div>哀与乐名也，闻与见亦名也，惑其名者失其实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1282163_comment'></div>是名即实，是实即名，名与实亦名也，惑其名者失其实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1282163_comment'></div>志即诗，诗即礼，礼即乐，乐即哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1282163_comment'></div>志气即天地，谓之充塞，非过论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1282163_comment'></div>谓天地合德可也，谓范围天地可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1282163_comment'></div>其曰「充塞」，乃因人心狭，固井蛙不可以骤语海，姑为是言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1282163_comment'></div>圣人之言，不可以一定论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1282163_comment'></div>或曰礼乐之原，或曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_105_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/282/Comments/0")'>五至</span>，或曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_105_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/283/Comments/0")'>三无</span>，或曰致，或曰行，纵而言之，错而论之，无不可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1282163_comment'></div>圣人曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_106_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/289/Comments/0")'>五至</span>，吾曰六曰七可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1282163_comment'></div>圣人曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_107_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/291/Comments/0")'>三无</span>，吾曰四曰五可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1282163_comment'></div>诗与礼与乐类也，忽继之以哀，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1282163_comment'></div>深明夫一体无二，纵而言之，错而论之，无不可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1282163_comment'></div>是故无声之乐即<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_110_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/300/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_110_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/301/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼即<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_110_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/301/Comments/1")'>无服之丧</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1282163_comment'></div>乐未尝无声，必曰无声，非无声也，即声也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1282163_comment'></div>礼未尝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/306/Comments/0")'>无体</span>，必曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/307/Comments/0")'>无体</span>，非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/308/Comments/0")'>无体</span>也，即体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1282163_comment'></div>丧未尝无服，必曰无服，非无服也，即服也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1282163_comment'></div>声即无声，体即<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_114_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/315/Comments/0")'>无体</span>，服即无服，本无所异，何必言同？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1282163_comment'></div>惟人徒执其声，故曰无声；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1282163_comment'></div>徒执其体，故曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_116_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/322/Comments/0")'>无体</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1282163_comment'></div>徒执其服，故曰无服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1282163_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「夙夜基命宥密」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1282163_comment'></div>命何所基？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1282163_comment'></div>命何所始？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1282163_comment'></div>始无所始，无所穷际，谓之极宽极宥可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1282163_comment'></div>不可得而见，不可得而闻，不可得而思，谓之至密可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1282163_comment'></div>曰基，曰宥，曰密，皆名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1282163_comment'></div>惑其名者，失其实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1282163_comment'></div>声即无声，天下之至实也，而徇名与声者惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1282163_comment'></div>圣人曰无声，所以破学者牢不可破之定见也，非以无声为定论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1282163_comment'></div>又虑学者无从而求之，使穷其本，始得其始，则得其终矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1282163_comment'></div>曰「基命」，所以原始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1282163_comment'></div>原声所始，始无所止，莫究厥始，莫穷厥终，莫执厥中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1282163_comment'></div>无声之乐，日闻四方，果日闻四方矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1282163_comment'></div>无声即声，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_131_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/363/Comments/0")'>无体</span>即体，无服即服，无本末，无粗精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1282163_comment'></div>威仪实<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_132_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/367/Comments/0")'>无体</span>，其曰「不可选也」，是诚不可选也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1282163_comment'></div>「凡民有丧，匍匐救之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1282163_comment'></div>是固<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_134_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/372/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>也，即齐、斩、功、缌之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1282163_comment'></div>于父斩衰，于母齐衰，兄弟期，降而功、缌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1282163_comment'></div>哀诚有等差，皆一心之为也，即匍匐救丧之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1282163_comment'></div>以丧其亲，则为齐、斩，为擗踊，为毁瘠，一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1282163_comment'></div>非人之所为也，天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1282163_comment'></div>天即人，人即天地，即日月，即四时，即鬼神，即礼乐之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1282163_comment'></div>原无所本，亦无所末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1282163_comment'></div>本末之名，因人心而生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1282163_comment'></div>本末之实，不以人心而异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1282163_comment'></div>人谓之本，则亦姑从而谓之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1282163_comment'></div>人谓之末，则亦姑从而谓之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1282163_comment'></div>人谓之天，则亦从而谓之天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1282163_comment'></div>人谓之地，则亦从而谓之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1282163_comment'></div>人曰日月，吾亦何得不谓之日月？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1282163_comment'></div>人曰四时，吾亦何得不谓之四时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1282163_comment'></div>人曰礼则曰礼，人曰乐则曰乐，人曰人则曰人，人曰道则曰道，曰气则曰气，曰志则曰志，曰有曰有，曰无曰无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1282163_comment'></div>号名纷然，意虑杂然，而未尝不浑然寂然也，人自以为纷然杂然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1282163_comment'></div>故曰即哀乐之相生，而实不可见，不可闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1282163_comment'></div>此非徇名者之所知也，亦非徇实者之所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1282163_comment'></div>实无所徇，实无所实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1282163_comment'></div>弃名而求实，非实也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1282163_comment'></div>弃实而言名，非名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1282163_comment'></div>实非学者之所知也，名亦非学者之所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1282163_comment'></div>知则不知，不知则知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1282163_comment'></div>知则乱，则昏，不知则清明，则无所不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1282163_comment'></div>孔子曰：「吾有知乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1282163_comment'></div>无知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1282163_comment'></div>文王「不识不知，顺帝之则」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1282163_comment'></div>子贡以为多学而识之，圣人以为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1282163_comment'></div>孔子又曰：「天下何思何虑」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1282163_comment'></div>学者茍有意焉，夫子必曰毋有必焉，必曰毋有固焉，必曰毋有我焉，必曰毋微有意象，如云气之蔽太虚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1282163_comment'></div>四方有败，安能先众人而知之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1282163_comment'></div>先知四方之败者，必其不识不知者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1282163_comment'></div>孔子曰「不逆诈，不亿不信」，而亦自先觉，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1282163_comment'></div>意虑不作，而本清本明之性自无所不照故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1282163_comment'></div>此非口舌之所能道也，此非思为之所能到也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1282163_comment'></div>人心自清，人心自明，人心自无思无为，人心自寂然不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1282163_comment'></div>思未尝思，人自以为思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1282163_comment'></div>为未尝为，人自以为为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1282163_comment'></div>清也，明也，无思也，无为也，寂然不动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1282163_comment'></div>知也，不知也，皆名也，惑其名者，失其实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1282163_comment'></div>子夏闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_175_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/488/Comments/0")'>三无</span>之论，曰：「言则大矣，美矣，盛矣，言尽于此而已乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1282163_comment'></div>是子夏未领吾圣人之旨也，圣人之旨非美盛所可得而言也，亦非言所可得而尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1282163_comment'></div>故孔子又启之曰，君子之服之也，又有五起焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1282163_comment'></div>服而念之，畅而明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1282163_comment'></div>五起，非有五者之不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1282163_comment'></div>五起犹五节，加焉而六可也，损焉而四亦可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1282163_comment'></div>纵而言之，错而论之，无不可者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1282163_comment'></div>无声之乐，气志不违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1282163_comment'></div>气志即乐，匪异匪违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_184_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/514/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，威仪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_184_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/515/Comments/0")'>迟迟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1282163_comment'></div>威仪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_185_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/516/Comments/0")'>迟迟</span>，不可度思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_186_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/518/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>，内恕孔悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1282163_comment'></div>其恕其悲，孰得而知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1282163_comment'></div>无声之乐，气志既得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1282163_comment'></div>得匪有得，亦匪无得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_190_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/526/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，威仪翼翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1282163_comment'></div>威仪翼翼，顺帝之则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_192_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/530/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>，施及四国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1282163_comment'></div>三者一旨，三者一德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1282163_comment'></div>无声之乐，气志既从，何异何同，昭明浑融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_195_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/538/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，上下和同，此敬此恭，何所不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_196_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/542/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>，以畜万邦，有安无危，有福无殃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1282163_comment'></div>无声之乐，日闻四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1282163_comment'></div>人皆闻之，而曰不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_199_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/550/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，日就月将，不勉不强，从容有常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_200_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/554/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>，纯德孔明，皓皓精白，礼乐同情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1282163_comment'></div>无声之乐，气志既起，斯起斯止，变化不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_202_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/562/Comments/0")'>无体</span>之礼，施及四海，此道大通，无远弗届。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1282163_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_203_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/566/Comments/0")'>无服之丧</span>，施于孙子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1282163_comment'></div>礼亦如此，乐亦如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1282163_comment'></div>三王之德如此，天地之德如此，日月之明如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1282163_comment'></div>天无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_206_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/573/Comments/0")'>私覆</span>，地无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_206_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/574/Comments/0")'>私载</span>，日月无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_206_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/575/Comments/0")'>私照</span>，人无私喜怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1282163_comment'></div>天地日月即人，人即天地日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1282163_comment'></div>以为异者，耳目思虑之所及也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1282163_comment'></div>以为同者，非耳目思虑之所及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1282163_comment'></div>非是有非，非及不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1282163_comment'></div>天人无违，故帝命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1282163_comment'></div>人而违天，私意作之，故天命去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1282163_comment'></div>得此道者谓之圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1282163_comment'></div>圣无不敬，敬非人为，是谓日跻，为则堕矣，莫克进矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1282163_comment'></div>进亦匪进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1282163_comment'></div>人言曰进，姑亦曰进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1282163_comment'></div>是进无思，是进无为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1282163_comment'></div>自然昭明，自然暇怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1282163_comment'></div>寂然浑然，融融<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_219_1282163", 1282163, "Clauses/604/Comments/0")'>迟迟</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1282163_comment'></div>所以顺帝则者在斯，所以作式于九围者在斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1282163_comment'></div>天有四时，春秋冬夏，风雨霜露，寂然浑然，其教我也昭然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1282163_comment'></div>自地而上，莫非神气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1282163_comment'></div>神气之可指者如风霆，风霆作而芽甲形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1282163_comment'></div>庶物露生，寂然浑然，其教我也昭然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1282163_comment'></div>其在我也，为百骸，为九窍，为视听言动，为气志嗜欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1282163_comment'></div>寂然浑然，又何其清明，又何其如神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1282163_comment'></div>即人即神，姑曰如神，何以验其神？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1282163_comment'></div>嗜欲将至，有开必先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1282163_comment'></div>天欲降雨，山川先云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1282163_comment'></div>宣王未出，而临莅天下也，而岳先降神，生甫及申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1282163_comment'></div>何为乎其神至如此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1282163_comment'></div>道通为一，其心甚神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1282163_comment'></div>神无方体，《易》曰「范围天地」，天地在吾心量中也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1282163_comment'></div>子思曰：「大哉，圣人之道，洋洋乎发育万物」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1282163_comment'></div>万物者圣人实发育之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1282163_comment'></div>此道非圣人独有而众人无也，天下之所同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1282163_comment'></div>自此而上，千万亿年皆此心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1282163_comment'></div>自此而下，千万亿年皆此心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1282163_comment'></div>天者，宣王之高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1282163_comment'></div>地者，宣王之博厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1282163_comment'></div>山川，宣王之流峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1282163_comment'></div>云雷风雨，宣王之震动散润。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1282163_comment'></div>嵩岳，宣王之嵩岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1282163_comment'></div>申甫，宣王之申甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1282163_comment'></div>在古不为先，在今不为今，在后不为后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1282163_comment'></div>浑然寂然，昭然不澄，治而常清，不思虑而常明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1282163_comment'></div>何独圣人为然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1282163_comment'></div>又何独宣王为然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1282163_comment'></div>乐平有老士王者，曩数年梦令遣胥致命，俾成先圣之宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1282163_comment'></div>且召之食，期日二十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1282163_comment'></div>至是默符曩梦，期日正同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1282163_comment'></div>故王老感异，捐金特盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1282163_comment'></div>此亦王老之有开必先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1282163_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1282163_comment'></div>人皆有是至灵至神、古今一贯之心，即天地之道，即礼乐之原，即文武之德，即三代之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1282163_comment'></div>而不知自贵，不知自爱，殊可念也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1282163_comment'></div>能自知者，千无一，万无一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1282163_comment'></div>自知诚鲜，而常知常明者又鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1282163_comment'></div>自知者，孔子谓之「知及之」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1282163_comment'></div>常知常明者，孔子谓之「仁能守之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1282163_comment'></div>自知非意虑之所及，亦非舍意虑之所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1282163_comment'></div>意虑交作，如四时之错行，如日月之代明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1282163_comment'></div>人皆有是明德，而不能以自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1282163_comment'></div>能自明而又不能常明，有时乎昏，则不可以为仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1282163_comment'></div>仁者觉之谓，医家者流谓四肢不觉为不仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1282163_comment'></div>先儒尝举此以明仁无一物之不觉，无一事之不觉，无斯须之不觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1282163_comment'></div>如日月中天，如水鉴昭明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1282163_comment'></div>常觉常明，自觉自明，昼夜通贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1282163_comment'></div>颜子进乎此，故曰「其心三月不违仁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1282163_comment'></div>其馀日月至者，如仲弓之徒，亦可以言仁，惟日月之外亦昏亦违，可以言仁，不可以言尽仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1282163_comment'></div>颜子几于尽仁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1282163_comment'></div>孔子六十而耳顺，则江汉以濯之，秋阳以暴之，皓皓乎不可尚已<span class='inlineComment2'>（《慈湖先生遗书续集》卷二。）</span>！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1282163_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_273_1282163'>此篇之前原尚有语录二则，其一则「学者当先读孔子之书」已见《遗书》卷一五《汎论学》篇，今删；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1282163_comment'></div>另一则「先生曰勿尽信非圣之书」今亦移于《汎论学》，此处删。</div><div id='poem_sentence_274_1282163_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1208&endYear=1208')">1208年4月28日</a>　四月二十三日，先生复熠书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1208&endYear=1208')">1208年夏</a>　夏，久旱得雨，诗呈张令君。作品：《湍水岩祷雨诗》<div id='poem_131304' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131304' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131304?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湍水岩祷雨诗<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1208年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_131304")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131304_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_131304_0'>① 戊辰之夏天久不雨农嗟失时孰不傍徨邑人余崇因干到县之石台乡遇一老人曰此地龙潭灵甚名湍水岩居士胡不祈于此崇回视间老人已不复见其神矣继到湍岩果是圣迹祷而归告于邑之士庶令君张君润之斋宿同诣潭所化龙随见甘雨沛然吾邑无不种之亩惠至渥也崇号湍岩居士一力经营刻立碑记装饰神像龙天感应岁斯上熟不可不记慈湖杨某</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131304'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131304'>湍水龙潭古迹遗，不因老叟有谁知。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131304_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131304'>乡人祷雨无灵日，云魃常旸尚在时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131304_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131304'>说与县家诚且信，去从潭所宿为期。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131304_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131304'>回头甘泽苏枯槁，插种工夫未是迟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131304_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131304'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131304_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_131245' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131245' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131245?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1208年夏）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_sentence_0_131245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131245'>驱除旱魃无馀事，感召灵神在寸忱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1210&endYear=1210')">1210年7月</a>　七月，记咏春堂。作品：《记》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明记文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1210&endYear=1210')">1210年</a>　有文，姑系于此。作品：《送子之官文》<div id='poem_1282104' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282104' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282104?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送子之官</a><span class='authorDate'>（1210年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282104")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282104_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282104'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282104'>尧、舜、禹皆圣人，犹相告以「执中」，又曰「惟精惟一」，又曰：「安女止」，而况于后学乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282104_comment'></div>女既于道有觉，又嗜欲淡薄，不以死生为畏，甚不易得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282104_comment'></div>皋陶犹曰：「兢兢业业」，女切宜克艰，以守中庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282104_comment'></div>此守非思虑言语所及，可惜可惜，敬之敬之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282104_comment'></div>兢业不兢业，即祸福荣辱之枢机。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1282104_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1210&endYear=1210')">1210年8月29日</a>　伯兄筹葬于此日，为撰墓志铭。作品：《宋杨公伯明封志》<span class='inlineComment2'>（“八月”年谱误为“日月”）</span><div id='poem_1282219' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282219' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282219?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨公伯明封志</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉定三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282219")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282219_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282219'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282219'>于乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282219_comment'></div>道非心思言论之所及，虽圣人不能强人之必明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282219_comment'></div>孔子大圣，其所启明，惟颜子三月不违，馀则日至月至，当是闵子骞、冉伯牛、仲弓、曾子诸贤，馀不能强也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282219_comment'></div>他日子夏、子张、子游以有若似圣人，欲以所事孔子事之，曾子曰：「不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282219_comment'></div>江汉以濯之，秋阳以暴之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282219_comment'></div>皓皓乎不可尚已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282219_comment'></div>厥后孟子得不学而能之良能，寥寥千载，无所考见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282219_comment'></div>我宋邵康节、程明道至矣，而偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282219_comment'></div>象山陆夫子生而清明，某先大夫颠沛而拱如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282219_comment'></div>伯兄讳筹字伯明，晚而顿觉，不勉不思，云为变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282219_comment'></div>易箦之言曰：「昔犹今，今犹昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282219_comment'></div>有能觉斯，随意而适」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282219_comment'></div>于乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282219_comment'></div>斯其庸，众所能知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282219_comment'></div>时嘉定三年二月庚申寿七十有八，□月甲申葬于慈溪县之石台乡句馀村孝顺里王岙先大夫墓左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282219_comment'></div>娶李氏，葬同域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282219_comment'></div>子：恬、惟、怟、慥、愉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282219_comment'></div>孟女归颜衮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282219_comment'></div>仲归舒钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282219_comment'></div>季归李竦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282219_comment'></div>孙圭至、学仲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282219_comment'></div>弟朝请郎、新差权发遣温州兼管内劝农事某兴哀起敬以书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1282219_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1215&endYear=1215')">1215年</a>　其领玉局而归，门人益亲。遐方僻峤，妇人孺子亦知有所谓慈湖先生岿然天地间，为斯文宗主，泰山乔岳，秋月独明。始传《古文孝经》、传《鲁论》，而厘正其篇次。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1216&endYear=1216')">1216年夏</a>　夏，有诗。作品：《丙子夏偶书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1217&endYear=1217')">1217年</a>　有诗。作品：《丁丑偶书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1217&endYear=1217')">1217年春</a>　春，有诗。作品：《丁丑咏春偶成》<div id='poem_131252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁丑咏春偶成<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1217年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_131252")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131252'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131252'>叶叶枝枝都教女，红红白白尽呈人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131252'>如何自古知音少，方到而今得句新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131217' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131217?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1219&endYear=1219')">1219年</a>　升直宝文阁，主管明道宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1219&endYear=1219')">1219年</a>　志钱子是妣徐氏墓。作品：《志》？<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1219&endYear=1219')">1219年</a>　季思请名其斋，简名之曰默，有文，姑系于本年。作品：《默斋记》<div id='poem_1282195' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282195' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282195?labeling=true' target='_blank'>默斋记<span class='inlineComment2'>（季思请名其斋，某名之曰「默」。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1219年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282195")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282195_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282195'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282195'>孔子曰「默而识之，学而不厌」，又曰「予欲无言」，又曰「吾有知乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282195_comment'></div>无知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282195_comment'></div>圣语昭然，而学者领圣人之旨者在孔门已甚无几，而况于后学乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282195_comment'></div>比来觉者何其多也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282195_comment'></div>觉非言语心思所及，季思已觉矣，汩于事而昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282195_comment'></div>孔子曰：「心之精神是谓圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282195_comment'></div>谓季思之心已圣，何不信圣训而复疑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282195_comment'></div>比日不复致问，季思以默识矣，季思平平守此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282195_comment'></div>默默即圣，即不厌之学，即喜怒哀乐之妙，即天地四时变化之妙，即先圣默识之妙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1282195_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1219&endYear=1219')">1219年</a>　撰《敬止记》<div id='poem_1282180' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282180' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282180?labeling=true' target='_blank'>敬止记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1219年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282180")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282180_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282180'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282180'>大人结茅家旁小山，先生命之曰「敬止」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282180_comment'></div>求说，先生曰：「敬止无说，某当为之记」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282180_comment'></div>明日授以此文，今附于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282180_comment'></div>槱敬书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282180_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1282180'>人有圣贤之异，道无圣贤之异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282180_comment'></div>孔子曰：「心之精神是谓圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282180_comment'></div>此心初无圣贤庸愚之间，百姓日用此心之妙而不自知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282180_comment'></div>禹曰「安女止」，本之不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282180_comment'></div>文王「缉熙敬止」，即不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282180_comment'></div>孔子「为之不厌」，岂未觉而为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282180_comment'></div>亦缉熙敬止，知及之后，观过精微，用力于仁守也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282180_comment'></div>如鉴中象，交错纷然，而虚明未尝有动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282180_comment'></div>子是知及，又进于仁守，兢兢钦哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1282180_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1219&endYear=1219')">1219年</a>　钱槱远访，从容近月，问答亦详矣。将归侍，复求言。有文。作品：《赠钱诚甫书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　除秘阁修撰，主管绍兴千秋鸿禧观。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1221&endYear=1221')">1221年</a>　邑令赵崇遂属乡先生杨简题纯德庙额。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1222&endYear=1222')">1222年</a>　特授朝请大夫、右文殿修撰，主管南京鸿庆宫，赐紫衣金鱼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1223&endYear=1223')">1223年</a>　进宝谟阁待制、提举鸿庆宫，赐金带。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1223&endYear=1223')">1223年</a>　陈埙丁父丧，从慈湖读礼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1224&endYear=1224')">1224年9月12日</a>　此日，理宗即位，进宝谟阁直学士，提举南京鸿庆宫，赐金带。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1224&endYear=1224')">1224年12月14日</a>　袁燮葬于此日，为撰墓志铭。作品：《志》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明志文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1224&endYear=1224')">1224年</a>　忠定之孙子仁复请文元讲学，故其居碧沚甚久。子仁受文元之教，终身不应召命。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1225&endYear=1225')">1225年</a>　宝庆元年，转朝议大夫、慈溪县男，寻授华文阁直学士、提举佑神观，奉朝请。诏入见，简屡辞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1225&endYear=1225')">1225年</a>　志臧孺人蒋氏墓。作品：《志》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明志文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年</a>　授敷文阁直学士，累加中大夫，仍提举鸿庆宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年</a>　寻升宝谟阁学士、太中大夫致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年3月23日</a>　此日卒，赠正奉大夫。<br /></div>
-----end

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年2月28日</a>　二月二十八日，杨简上疏留汝愚，李沐又劾之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1208&endYear=1210')">1208-1210年</a>，68-70岁</div><div id='c4107817f19548d2a57758d1424f5ecc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1208&endYear=1208')">1208年12月</a>　授秘书郞，转朝请郞，迁秘书省著作佐郞兼权兵部郞官。十二月，转对，极言经国之要，弭灾厉、消祸变之道，北境传诵，为之涕泣。<br /><a href="javascript: class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明文章名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1208&endYear=1208')">1208年</a>　奠高处约，姑系于本年。作品：《奠辞》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明文章名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1209')">1209年3月</a>　三月，撰《著庭记》<div id='poem_1282185' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282185' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282185?labeling=true' target='_blank'>著庭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1209年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282185")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282185_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282185'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282185'>孔子曰：「属辞比事，《春秋》教也」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282185_comment'></div>「属辞比事而不乱，则深于《春秋》者矣」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282185_comment'></div>「天有四时，春秋冬夏，风雨霜露，无非教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282185_comment'></div>地载神气，神气风霆，风霆流形，庶物露生，无非教也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282185_comment'></div>某不胜起敬，而赞之曰：大哉圣言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282185_comment'></div>著庭以属辞比事为职，辞不胜其繁，事不胜其夥，何以不乱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282185_comment'></div>乱生于意，意生纷然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282185_comment'></div>意如云气，能障太虚之清明，能蔽日月之光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282185_comment'></div>舜曰「道心」，明心即道，动乎意则为人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282185_comment'></div>孔子曰：「心之精神是谓圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282185_comment'></div>而每戒学者「毋意，毋必，毋固，毋我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282185_comment'></div>意态万殊，而大槩无踰斯四者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282185_comment'></div>圣人深知意之害道也甚，故谆谆止绝学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282185_comment'></div>门弟子欲尽记之，则不胜其记，故总而记之曰「子绝四」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282185_comment'></div>动乎意者必谓属辞比事如此，春秋冬夏、风雨霜露如彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282185_comment'></div>属辞比事如此，若之何而一？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282185_comment'></div>《易》曰「艮其背」，背尚不知其为一，而况于不一？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282185_comment'></div>「不识不知，是谓帝则」，圣人曰「中庸」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282185_comment'></div>庸，常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282185_comment'></div>明夫日用平常之心，何思何虑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282185_comment'></div>虚明无体，广大无际，天地范围于其中，四时运行于其中，风霆雨露雪霜动散于其中，万物发育于其中，辞生于其中，事生于其中，属而比之于其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282185_comment'></div>如镜中象，虽纷扰参错，而未尝动也，不可以为有也，而亦不可以为无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282185_comment'></div>不可度思，矧可射思？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282185_comment'></div>《春秋》之大义在斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282185_comment'></div>嘉定二年窉月，朝请郎、行秘书省著作佐郎、兼兵部郎官杨某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1282185_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1209')">1209年5月11日</a>　此日，铭邹鲁卿墓。作品：《邹鲁卿墓铭》<div id='poem_1282213' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282213' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282213?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邹鲁卿墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉定二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282213")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282213_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282213'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282213'>某为乐平，首得邹梦遇，某字之曰元祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282213_comment'></div>元祥自有觉，某从而涤其滓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282213_comment'></div>元祥之叔祖居德兴，名近仁，字鲁卿，又来访道，某与语从容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282213_comment'></div>翼日又与语良久，忽觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282213_comment'></div>厥后数款语益信其果觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282213_comment'></div>嘉定二年春至行都，又从容累日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282213_comment'></div>归未几而疾作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282213_comment'></div>仲夏癸卯，忽盥手，振衣而坐，召子曾曰：「吾心甚明，无事可言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282213_comment'></div>尔辈脩身学道，则为孝矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282213_comment'></div>言讫而瞑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282213_comment'></div>元祥以讣来，予哭于寝门之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282213_comment'></div>曾不惮脩途至，通名，予意鲁卿之子，已而问之，果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282213_comment'></div>予哭，曾哭而拜，予答拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282213_comment'></div>唁问既久，留终日，知曾因元祥而又觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282213_comment'></div>曾请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282213_comment'></div>其父墓在龙田山之阿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282213_comment'></div>鲁卿祖讳圣从，嘉州文学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282213_comment'></div>父讳孟，登进士科，初尉建德，后隆兴录参。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282213_comment'></div>鲁卿质直不事文饰，以孝闻，恶衣菲食，穷居而乐，和而敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282213_comment'></div>或干以非义，则介焉弗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282213_comment'></div>告以有过，则敛衽谢服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282213_comment'></div>所当为，虽强御弗畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282213_comment'></div>以特恩为静江法曹，再调龙阳丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282213_comment'></div>娶董氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282213_comment'></div>长子峄，次曾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282213_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1282213'>孔子殁，月至日至者又殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282213_comment'></div>谁其嗣之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282213_comment'></div>孟入圣域，濂溪、明道似之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282213_comment'></div>象山陆子则有之，鲁卿同之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1282213_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1209')">1209年5月27日</a>　此日，诏以旱蝗求直言，简上封事，言旱蝗根本，近在人心。兼考功郞官，兼礼部郞官,授著作郞、将作少监。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1209')">1209年</a>　史弥忠以慈湖荐宰庐陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1209')">1209年8月</a>　八月，书“参前”二字，又记。作品：《记》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明记文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1209&endYear=1209')">1209年9月10日</a>　此日，明堂礼成，献诗，未上。作品：《诗》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明诗名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1214&endYear=1214')">1214年</a>　金人大饥，来归者日以数千、万计，边吏临淮水射之。先生戚然，即日上奏，言之，不报。会有疾，请去益力，直宝谟阁主管成都府玉局观。<br /></div>

-----title
富阳

-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6c4288b0037e41f9a0083bbc077d63ec_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6c4288b0037e41f9a0083bbc077d63ec");'><span id='6c4288b0037e41f9a0083bbc077d63ec_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　为绍兴府司理，犴狱必亲临，端默以听，使自吐露。越陪都，台府鼎立，简中立无颇，惟理之从。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年1月1日</a>　元日，有文，姑系于本年。作品：《释菜祭文》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　有文，姑系于本年。作品：《秋祀禹庙文》《晋王右军祠祝文》<div id='poem_1282264' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282264' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282264?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋祀禹庙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1177年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282264")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282264_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282264'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282264'>某不可思，克艰若时，精一专钦，惟圣帝道光，万世赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282264_comment'></div>秋有彝章，酌献豆觞。<div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282265'>右军偃武正论，百世不磨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282265_comment'></div>字画累我，顾为惭德者所多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282265_comment'></div>后儒罕知治道，往往以俎豆之事，老生常谈，而翰墨潇洒骏逸之态，争睹欣玩，袂相属，肩相摩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282265_comment'></div>今兹针群子之膏肓，障千载之颓波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282265_comment'></div>右将军本衷清明，当知后世有四明杨某者发其正情。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1282265_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宁波（鄞县）
-----detail
