-----title
乐平
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c923c64bc16f4841bf3215faaee86b66_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c923c64bc16f4841bf3215faaee86b66");'><span id='c923c64bc16f4841bf3215faaee86b66_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1193')">1192-1193年</a>，52-53岁</div><div id='c923c64bc16f4841bf3215faaee86b66' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年闰2月1日</a>　此日，知乐平县。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　兴学训士，诸生闻其言，有泣下者。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　杨、石二少年为民害，简置狱中，谕以祸福，咸感悟，愿自赎。由是邑人以讼为耻，夜无盗警，路不拾遗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年8月</a>　是月，撰《乐平县重修社坛记》<div id='poem_1282196' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282196' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282196?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乐平县重修社坛记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282196")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282196_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282196'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282196'>国有常典，守令首谒社稷，视坛壝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282196_comment'></div>绍熙三年春二月闰朔，县令杨某既领事，命新县社之门与其庭，而修筑其墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282196_comment'></div>财计匮乏，虽弗克极其宏壮，而不敢不敬之意于是乎在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282196_comment'></div>仲秋讫工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282196_comment'></div>某仰惟国家崇敬社稷，厥有大义，至高至深，至神至明，未有发挥其蕴，昭示今后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282196_comment'></div>某偶当其职，任其事，不敢逊，乃起敬起恭，从容秉笔而书曰：夫社谓夫土之有神也，稷谓夫百谷之生有神也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282196_comment'></div>其祀事则二，其神道则一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282196_comment'></div>子思曰：「天地之道，其为物不贰，则其生物不测」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282196_comment'></div>孔子曰：「地载神气，神气风霆，风霆流形，庶物露生，无非教也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282196_comment'></div>又曰：「吾道一以贯之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282196_comment'></div>皆所以明著至神之道，无不通贯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282196_comment'></div>惟神不形，惟神不名，天以是健行，地以是发生，人以是灵，百谷草木以是成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282196_comment'></div>莫究厥始，莫穷厥终，故夫无思无为，寂然不动，感而遂通，三才之所同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282196_comment'></div>变化云为，不疾而速，不行而至，三才之所同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282196_comment'></div>曰阴曰阳，举不得而测，三才之所同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282196_comment'></div>道在迩而求诸远，事在易而求诸难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282196_comment'></div>人心诚实无他，本体清明，本用神明，刚健中正，纯粹精一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282196_comment'></div>乾元在斯，坤元在斯，有感有应，无不通矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282196_comment'></div>祀典修兴，神道著矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282196_comment'></div>笾豆斯设，奠荐斯行，不可度思，矧可射思！</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1282196_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年2月1日</a>　此日，遣奠孙明仲，有文。作品：《慈湖遗书·祭孙元礼尊人文》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　新乐平县学成，记之。作品：《乐平县学记》<div id='poem_1282172' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282172' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282172?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乐平县学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282172")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282172_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282172'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282172'>绍熙三年二月闰朔，某始领邑事，敬瞻先圣之宫隘陋甚，无以起人崇敬之心，思撤而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282172_comment'></div>县计大匮，不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282172_comment'></div>同官协谋，邑人丕应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282172_comment'></div>越明年，中殿崇成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282172_comment'></div>戟门前峙，修廊翼之，因廊为斋，学者有安居之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282172_comment'></div>惟讲道之堂仍其旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282172_comment'></div>某惟先圣所以佑启后学之意，岂徒事文貌、为讲说而已？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282172_comment'></div>人咸有良性，清明未尝不在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282172_comment'></div>人欲蔽之，如云翳日，是故不可无学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282172_comment'></div>学非外求，人心自善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282172_comment'></div>孩提皆知爱亲及长，皆知敬兄，不学而能，不虑而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282172_comment'></div>人心自仁，大道在我，无所不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282172_comment'></div>圣人曰「时习」，明其无时而不习也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282172_comment'></div>无时而不习，非学而能、虑而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282172_comment'></div>有所思焉，思有时而止；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282172_comment'></div>有所为焉，为有时而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282172_comment'></div>匪思匪为，匪合匪离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282172_comment'></div>孝弟之至，通于神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282172_comment'></div>其与人为忠，其恕人为恕，其节为礼，其和为乐，其知为智，名殊而道同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282172_comment'></div>意虑不作，其学常通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282172_comment'></div>清明有融，故乐生其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282172_comment'></div>夫孰得其所始，又孰穷其所终？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282172_comment'></div>圣人谓时习而说，斯可言学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282172_comment'></div>苟未能无时而不习，有斯须之违焉，不可以言学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282172_comment'></div>或自以为时习矣，有滞留之意，无油然之乐，亦不可以言学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282172_comment'></div>时习而说，此善学之验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282172_comment'></div>大哉圣言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282172_comment'></div>洞照学者心术之隐微，万世不可违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282172_comment'></div>其有违者，所学必非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282172_comment'></div>千失万过，孰不由意虑而生乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282172_comment'></div>意动于爱恶，故有过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282172_comment'></div>意动于声色，故有过；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282172_comment'></div>意动于云为，故有过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1282172_comment'></div>意无所动，本亦无过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1282172_comment'></div>先圣所以每每止绝学者之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1282172_comment'></div>门弟子总记之曰「毋意」，为是故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1282172_comment'></div>从游三千，独曰颜子好学，日至月至者不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1282172_comment'></div>何谓至？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1282172_comment'></div>至，止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1282172_comment'></div>《书》曰：「安女止」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1282172_comment'></div>良性寂然，清明而不动，自知自信，自清自明，自寂自止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1282172_comment'></div>虽万变万化，交扰参错，而实无所动，故曰至，又曰止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1282172_comment'></div>至矣止矣，何以学为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1282172_comment'></div>吁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1282172_comment'></div>本心虽明，故习尚熟，微蔽尚有，意虑萌蘖，即与道违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1282172_comment'></div>道不我违，我自违道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1282172_comment'></div>有我有违，无我无违；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1282172_comment'></div>有我斯动，无我则无动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1282172_comment'></div>我本无我，意立而成我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1282172_comment'></div>日至之外犹有违，意起而动故也，月至则益熟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1282172_comment'></div>月至之外犹有违，亦意起而动故也，至于颜子三月不违，益精益一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1282172_comment'></div>三月而往，犹微有违，不远而复，纯一如故，不动如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1282172_comment'></div>变化云为，皓皓精白，是谓「时习而说」之学，是谓「文王之德之纯」，是谓「惟精惟一，允执厥中」，是谓「吾道一以贯之」，是谓天下万世生民自有之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1282172_comment'></div>具衔杨某谨记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1282172_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年6月9日</a>　六月九日，撰《二陆先生祠堂记》<div id='poem_1282176' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282176' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282176?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二陆先生祠记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年6月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282176")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282176_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282176'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282176'>道心大同，人自区别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282176_comment'></div>人心自善，人心自灵，人心自明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282176_comment'></div>人心即神，人心即道，安睹乖殊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282176_comment'></div>圣贤非有馀，愚鄙非不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282176_comment'></div>何以證其然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282176_comment'></div>人皆有恻隐之心，皆有羞恶之心，皆有恭敬之心，皆有是非之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282176_comment'></div>恻隐，仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282176_comment'></div>羞恶，义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282176_comment'></div>恭敬，礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282176_comment'></div>是非，知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282176_comment'></div>仁义礼知，愚夫愚妇咸有之，奚独圣贤有之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282176_comment'></div>人人皆与尧、舜、禹、汤、文、武、周公、孔子同，人人皆与天地同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282176_comment'></div>又何以證其然？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282176_comment'></div>人心非气血，非形体，广大无际，变化无方，倏焉而视，又倏焉而听，倏焉而言，又倏焉而动，倏焉而至千里之外，又倏焉而穷九霄之上，不疾而速，不行而至，非神乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282176_comment'></div>不与天地同乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282176_comment'></div>学者当知，举天下万古之人心皆如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282176_comment'></div>孔子之心如此，七十子之心如此，子思、孟子之心如此，复斋之心如此，象山先生之心如此，金溪王令君之心如此，举金溪一邑之心如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282176_comment'></div>学者当自信，毋自弃，毋自疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282176_comment'></div>意虑倏起，天地悬隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282176_comment'></div>不识不知，匪合匪离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282176_comment'></div>直心而往，自备万善，自绝百非，虽无思为，昭明弗遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282176_comment'></div>二陆先生，抚州金溪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282176_comment'></div>复斋讳九龄，字子寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282176_comment'></div>笃志斯道，穷深究微，兢兢孜孜，学者宗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282176_comment'></div>象山先生其弟也，讳九渊，字子静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282176_comment'></div>天性清明，不染物欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282176_comment'></div>某尝亲闻先生之言，自谓其为童幼时，闻人诵伊川语，自觉若伤我者，性资素明如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282176_comment'></div>故长而益明，愈久而愈明，破学者于窟宅，开圣道之夷涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282176_comment'></div>其言甚平，而或者填万说于胸中，持万说于胸中以听先生之言，故或疑其深，疑其峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282176_comment'></div>然而海内之士闻其风而趋之，如百川之东矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282176_comment'></div>某积疑二十年，先生一语触其机，某始自信其心之即道，而非有二物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282176_comment'></div>始信天下之人心皆与尧、舜、禹、汤、文、武、周公、孔子同，皆与天地日月四时鬼神同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282176_comment'></div>王令君名有大，因邑人崇敬二君子，以俸资设祠于学，且将行礼焉，属某为记，且曰：「欲以昭明二君子之道」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1282176_comment'></div>某虽无所似，灼知二君子之心无以异于天下之心，不容穿凿其说，以滋惑来者，乃起敬起恭，而书其略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1282176_comment'></div>绍熙四年六月九日，门人具位杨某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1282176_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1282176'><span class='label'>按：</span>《慈湖先生遗书》卷二。又见宋李恭伯《象山先生年谱》，道光《金溪县志》卷五四。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1282176_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　自夏徂秋不雨，年谷大损。令杨简忧盗起，讲聚民之政，以关郊内自任。稍采乡誉，分乡职曰粜、曰贷、 曰济，次第具举。邑无可粜，责之民廪；邑无可贷，请之仓台；邑无可济，移之上供。岁虽饥，不害.有文。作品：《慈湖遗书·祈雨文》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　有诸庙《祈雨文》<div id='poem_1282291' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282291' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282291?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诸庙祈雨文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282291")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282291_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282291'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282291'>某兹以愆阳为灾，阖郡危惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282291_comment'></div>众祷虔虔，应亦累累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282291_comment'></div>檐溜已鸣，忽复告止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282291_comment'></div>农事甚急，过此无及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282291_comment'></div>某德未纯，某知罪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282291_comment'></div>惟神敷惠千里之氓，锡以三日之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282291_comment'></div>生死骨肉，判于旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282291_comment'></div>某不胜恳恳祷祷之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1282291_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　有诸庙《谢雨文》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　葺乐平主簿厅，为之记。作品：《记》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明记文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年10月</a>　十月，裘万顷任主簿，初见长官杨简，拜为道徳师。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='175fcd64d93f4295a883db7513939e9f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("175fcd64d93f4295a883db7513939e9f");'><span id='175fcd64d93f4295a883db7513939e9f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>，54岁</div><div id='175fcd64d93f4295a883db7513939e9f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年2月</a>　二月，撰《王珪节庵记》<div id='poem_1282189' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282189' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282189?labeling=true' target='_blank'>节庵记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282189")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282189_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282189'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282189'>州曰饶，县曰乐平，乡曰怀义，山曰金银，庵曰节居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282189_comment'></div>其庵者曰玉甫，其姓王，其名圭，今或字曰羲民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282189_comment'></div>问其所以名庵之义，曰：「叔南安名之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282189_comment'></div>其说曰：竹有节，不可改易，霜莫能凌，雪莫能凋，欲玉甫之守清节不移也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282189_comment'></div>属某发挥其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282189_comment'></div>玉甫所自有，自不可改，奚俟某发挥？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282189_comment'></div>然庵之左后有松焉，山风入松，萧然有声，此足以发挥其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282189_comment'></div>其南有陂流焉，波流湍鸣，泠泠其音，足以发挥其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282189_comment'></div>环庵皆茂林，山禽鸣声，足以发挥其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282189_comment'></div>斯义可闻而不可言，可言而不可思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282189_comment'></div>玉甫之节如此，某之节如此，天地之节如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282189_comment'></div>绍熙甲寅仲春四明杨某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1282189_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年2月16日</a>　二月十六日，撰《象山行状》<div id='poem_1282205' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282205' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282205?labeling=true' target='_blank'>象山先生行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年2月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282205")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282205_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282205'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282205'>先生姓陆，名九渊，字子静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282205_comment'></div>其先妫姓，至齐宣王少子元侯讳通始封平原般县陆乡，因以为氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282205_comment'></div>曾孙讳烈，为吴令，子孙遂为吴郡吴县人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282205_comment'></div>自吴令四十世为唐宰相文公讳希声，是为先生八世祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282205_comment'></div>七世祖讳崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282205_comment'></div>六世祖讳德迁，五代末避地于抚州金溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282205_comment'></div>高祖讳有程，曾祖讳演，并以学行重于乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282205_comment'></div>祖讳戬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282205_comment'></div>父赠宣教郎讳贺，生有异禀，端重不伐，究心典籍，见于躬行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282205_comment'></div>酌先儒冠昏丧祭之礼，行之家，家道之整，著闻州里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282205_comment'></div>母孺人饶氏，生六子，先生其季也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282205_comment'></div>先生幼不喜弄，静重如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282205_comment'></div>三四岁时常侍宣教公行，遇事物必致问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282205_comment'></div>一日忽问天地何所穷际，宣教公笑而不答，遂深思至忘寝食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282205_comment'></div>角总经夕不脱衣，履有敝而无坏，袜至三接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282205_comment'></div>手甲甚修，足迹未尝至庖厨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282205_comment'></div>常自扫洒林下，宴坐终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282205_comment'></div>立于门，过者驻望称叹，以其端庄雍容异常儿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282205_comment'></div>五岁读书，纸隅无捲摺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282205_comment'></div>六岁侍亲，会嘉礼，衣以华好，却不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282205_comment'></div>季兄复斋，年十三，举礼经以告先生，乃受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282205_comment'></div>与人粹然乐易，然恶无礼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282205_comment'></div>读书不苟简，外视虽若閒暇，而实勤于考索。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282205_comment'></div>伯兄总家务，常夜分起，必见先生秉烛检书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282205_comment'></div>伊川近世大儒，言垂于后，至今学者尊敬讲习之不替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282205_comment'></div>先生独谓某曰：「丱角时闻人诵伊川语，自觉若伤我者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282205_comment'></div>亦尝谓人曰：「伊川之言奚为与孔子、孟子之言不类」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282205_comment'></div>初读《论语》，即疑有子之言支离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282205_comment'></div>先生生而清明，不可企及，有如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282205_comment'></div>他日读古书至「宇宙」二字，解者曰四方上下曰宇，往古来今曰宙，忽大省曰：「宇宙内事乃己分内事，己分内事乃宇宙内事」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282205_comment'></div>又尝曰：「东海有圣人出焉，此心同也，此理同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282205_comment'></div>西海有圣人出焉，此心同也，此理同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282205_comment'></div>南海北海有圣人出焉，此心同也，此理同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1282205_comment'></div>千百世之上有圣人出焉，此心同也，此理同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1282205_comment'></div>千百世之下有圣人出焉，此心同也，此理同也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1282205_comment'></div>乾道八年登进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1282205_comment'></div>时考官吕祖谦能识先生之文于数千人之中，他日谓先生曰：「未尝款承足下之教，仅得之传闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1282205_comment'></div>一见高文，心开目明，知其为江西陆子静也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1282205_comment'></div>其始至行都，一时俊杰咸从之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1282205_comment'></div>先生朝夕应酬答问，学者踵至，至不得寐者馀四十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1282205_comment'></div>所以自奉甚薄，而精神益强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1282205_comment'></div>听其言，兴起者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1282205_comment'></div>还里，远迩闻风而至，求亲炙问道者益盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1282205_comment'></div>先生既受徒，即去今世所谓学规者，而诸生善心自兴，容体自庄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1282205_comment'></div>雍雍于于，后至者相观而化，猗欤盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1282205_comment'></div>真三代时学校也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1282205_comment'></div>有一生饭次微交足，饭既，先生从容问之曰：「汝适有过，知之乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1282205_comment'></div>生略思曰：「已省」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1282205_comment'></div>先生曰：「何过」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1282205_comment'></div>对曰：「中食觉交足，虽即改正，亦放逸也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1282205_comment'></div>其严如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1282205_comment'></div>先生深知学者心术之微，言中其情，或至汗下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1282205_comment'></div>有怀于中而不能自晓者，为之条析其故，悉如其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1282205_comment'></div>亦有相去千里，素无雅故，闻其大概而尽得其为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1282205_comment'></div>尝有言曰：「念虑之不正者，顷刻而知之，即可以正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1282205_comment'></div>念虑之正者，顷刻而失之，即为不正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1282205_comment'></div>有可以形迹观者，有不可以形迹观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1282205_comment'></div>必以形迹观人，则不足以知人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1282205_comment'></div>必以形迹绳人，则不足以救人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1282205_comment'></div>又曰：「今天下学者唯有两途：一途朴实，一途议论」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1282205_comment'></div>呜呼，至哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1282205_comment'></div>足以明人心之邪正，破学者之窟宅矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1282205_comment'></div>尝攻切问者之疵，问者不领，恶声辄至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1282205_comment'></div>旁观不能堪，而先生悠然从容，乃及他事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1282205_comment'></div>淳熙元年，授迪功郎、隆兴府靖安县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1282205_comment'></div>未上，丁继母太孺人邓氏忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1282205_comment'></div>服阕，调建宁府崇安县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1282205_comment'></div>八年，少师史公浩荐先生之辞曰：「渊源之学，沈粹之行，辈行推之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1282205_comment'></div>而心悟理融，出于自得」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1282205_comment'></div>得旨，都堂审察，升擢，不赴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1282205_comment'></div>九年，侍从复上荐，除国子正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1282205_comment'></div>诸生叩请，孳孳启谕，如家居教授，感发良多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1282205_comment'></div>十年冬，迁敕令所删定官，同志之士相从讲切不替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1282205_comment'></div>僚友多贤，相与问辨，大信服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1282205_comment'></div>先生自少时闻长上道靖康间事，慨然有感于复雠之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1282205_comment'></div>至是遂访求智勇之士与之商榷，益知武事利病，形势要害，人物短长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1282205_comment'></div>十一年，当轮对，期迫甚，犹未入思虑，所亲屡请，久乃下笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1282205_comment'></div>缮写甫就，厥明，即对上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1282205_comment'></div>屡俞所奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1282205_comment'></div>脩宽恤诏令，书成，有旨改承奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1282205_comment'></div>十三年，转宣义郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1282205_comment'></div>亲朋谓先生久次，宜求去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1282205_comment'></div>先生曰：「往时面对，粗陈大义，明主不以为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1282205_comment'></div>然条贯靡竟，统纪未终，思欲再望清光，少自竭尽，以致臣子之义」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1282205_comment'></div>距对五日，除将作监丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1282205_comment'></div>后省疏駮，得旨，主管台州崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1282205_comment'></div>先生既归，学者辐辏愈盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1282205_comment'></div>虽乡曲老长亦俯首听诲言，称先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1282205_comment'></div>先生悼时俗之通病，启人心之固有，咸惕然以惩，跃然以兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1282205_comment'></div>每诣城邑，环坐率一二百人，至不能容，徙观寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1282205_comment'></div>县大夫为设讲坐于学宫，听者贵贱老少溢塞涂巷，从游之盛，未见有此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1282205_comment'></div>贵溪有山，实龙虎之本冈，先生登而乐之，结茅其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1282205_comment'></div>山高五里，其形如象，遂名之曰象山，自号象山翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1282205_comment'></div>四方学徒复大集，至数百人，从容讲道，咏歌怡愉，有终焉之意，于是人号象山先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1282205_comment'></div>十六年，祠秩满，今上登极，除知荆门军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1282205_comment'></div>是年转宣教郎，又转奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1282205_comment'></div>绍熙二年九月初领郡事，吏以故例白内诸局务、外诸县必有揭示约束，接宾受词分日，先生曰：「安用是」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1282205_comment'></div>延见僚属如朋友，推心豁然，论事惟理是从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1282205_comment'></div>先生家书有云：「每一同官禀事，众有所见，皆得展其所怀，辩争利害于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1282205_comment'></div>太守惟默听，俟其是非既明，乃从赞叹，以养其徇公之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1282205_comment'></div>太守所判，僚属却回者常有之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1282205_comment'></div>先生教民如子弟，虽贱隶走卒亦谕以理义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1282205_comment'></div>接宾受词无早暮，下情尽达无壅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1282205_comment'></div>故郡境之内官吏之贪廉，民俗之习尚，忠良材武与猾吏暴强，先生皆得之于无事之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1282205_comment'></div>往时郡有追逮，皆特遣人，先生惟令诉者自执状以追，以地近远立限，皆如期，即日处决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1282205_comment'></div>轻罪多酌人情晓令解释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1282205_comment'></div>至人伦之讼既明，多使领原词自毁之，以厚其俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1282205_comment'></div>惟怙终不可诲化，乃始断治，详其文状，以防后日反覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1282205_comment'></div>久之民情益孚，两造有不持状，惟对辩求决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1282205_comment'></div>亦有證者不召自至，问其故，曰：「事久不白，共约求明」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1282205_comment'></div>或既伏，俾各持其状去，不复留案。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1282205_comment'></div>尝夜与僚属坐，吏白有老者诉甚急，呼问之，体战，言不可解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1282205_comment'></div>俾吏状之，谓其子为群卒所杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1282205_comment'></div>先生判翌日呈，僚属难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1282205_comment'></div>先生曰：「子安之，不至是」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1282205_comment'></div>凌晨追究其子，盖无恙也，人益服先生之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1282205_comment'></div>有诉遭窃脱，而不知其人，先生自出二人姓名，使捕至，讯之，伏辜，尽得所窃物还诉者，且宥其罪，使自新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1282205_comment'></div>因语吏曰：「某所某人尤暴」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1282205_comment'></div>吏亦莫知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1282205_comment'></div>翌日有诉遭夺掠者，即其人也，乃加追治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1282205_comment'></div>吏大惊，郡人以为神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1282205_comment'></div>初，保伍之制，州县以非急务，多不检覈，盗贼得匿藏其间，近边尤以为患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1282205_comment'></div>先生首申严之，奸无所蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1282205_comment'></div>有劫僧庐，邻伍遽集擒获，不逸一人，至是群盗屏息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1282205_comment'></div>荆门素无城壁，先生以为此自古战争之场，今为次边，在江汉之间，为四集之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1282205_comment'></div>南捍江陵，北援襄阳，东护随、郢之胁，西当光化、夷陵之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1282205_comment'></div>荆门固，则四邻有所恃，否则有背胁腹心之虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1282205_comment'></div>由唐之湖阳以趋山，则其涉汉之径，已在荆门之胁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1282205_comment'></div>由邓之邓城以涉汉，则其趋山之道已在荆门之腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1282205_comment'></div>馀有间途浅津，坡陁不能限马，滩濑不能以濡轨者，所在尚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1282205_comment'></div>自我出奇制胜，徼敌兵之腹胁者亦正在此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1282205_comment'></div>虽四山环合，易于备御，义勇四千强壮可用，而仓廪藏库之间麋鹿可至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1282205_comment'></div>累政欲脩筑子城，惮重费不敢轻举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1282205_comment'></div>先生审度决计，召集义勇，优给佣直，躬自劝督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1282205_comment'></div>役者乐趋竭力，工倍，二旬讫筑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1282205_comment'></div>初计者拟费缗钱二十万，至是仅费缗五千而土工毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1282205_comment'></div>后复议成砌三重，置角台，增二小门，上置敌楼，冲天渠、荷叶渠、护险墙之制毕备，才费缗钱三万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1282205_comment'></div>又郡学贡院、客馆、官舍众役并兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1282205_comment'></div>初，俗习惰，人以执役为耻，吏惟好衣閒观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1282205_comment'></div>至是风一变，督役官吏布衣杂役夫佐力，相勉以义，不专以威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1282205_comment'></div>盛役如此，而人情晏然，郡中恬若无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1282205_comment'></div>荆门两县置垒，事力绵薄，连岁困于送迎，藏库空竭，调度倚办商税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1282205_comment'></div>先是，日差使臣暨小吏伺商人于门，检货给引，然后至务，务惟据引入税，出门又覆视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1282205_comment'></div>官收无几，而出入其费已多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1282205_comment'></div>初谓以严禁榷杜奸弊，而门吏取贿，多所藏覆，禁物亦或通行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1282205_comment'></div>商苦重费，多由僻途，务入日缩，先生罢去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1282205_comment'></div>或曰：「关讥所以防奸，列郡行之以为常，一旦罢废，商冒利，必有不至务者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1282205_comment'></div>先生曰：「是非尔所知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1282205_comment'></div>即日揭示，俾径至务，复减正税援例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1282205_comment'></div>是日税入立增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1282205_comment'></div>有一巨商已遵僻途，忽闻新令，复出正路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1282205_comment'></div>巡尉卒于歧捕之，先生诘得其实，劳而释之，巨商感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1282205_comment'></div>行旅闻者莫不以手加额，誓以毋欺私相转告，必由荆门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1282205_comment'></div>旁观者诘其故，商曰：「罢三门，引减援例，去我辈大害，不可不报德」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1282205_comment'></div>税收增倍，酒课亦如之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1282205_comment'></div>荆门故用铜钱，后以近边，以铁钱易之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1282205_comment'></div>铜钱有禁，而民之输于公者尚容贴纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1282205_comment'></div>先生曰：「既禁之矣，又使之输，不可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1282205_comment'></div>即蠲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1282205_comment'></div>又减钞钱，罢比较，不遣人诣县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1282205_comment'></div>给吏札，置医院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1282205_comment'></div>官吏民咸悦，而郡吏亦贫而乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1282205_comment'></div>狱卒无以自给，多告罢，先生以僚属访察得其实，遂廪给之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1282205_comment'></div>朔望及暇日诣学讲诲诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1282205_comment'></div>郡有故事，上元设斋醮黄堂，其说曰为民祈福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1282205_comment'></div>先生于是会吏民讲《洪范》敛福锡民一章以代醮事，发明人心之善，所以自求多福者莫不晓然，有感于中，或为之泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1282205_comment'></div>湖北诸郡军士多逃徙，视官府如传舍，不可禁止，缓急无可使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1282205_comment'></div>先生病之，乃信捕获之赏，重奔窜之刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1282205_comment'></div>又数阅射，中者受赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1282205_comment'></div>役之加佣值，无饥寒之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1282205_comment'></div>相与悉心弓矢，逸者绝少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1282205_comment'></div>他日兵官按阅，独荆门整习，他郡所无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1282205_comment'></div>先生平时按射不止于兵伍，郡民皆得而与，中亦同赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1282205_comment'></div>荐举其属不限流品，尝曰：「古者无流品之分，而贤不肖之辨严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1282205_comment'></div>后世有流品之分，而贤不肖之辨略」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1282205_comment'></div>先生之家居也，乡人苦旱，群祷莫应，有请于先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1282205_comment'></div>乃除坛山巅，除已，云交，及致祷，大雨随至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1282205_comment'></div>荆门亦旱，先生每有祈必疏雨随车，郡民异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1282205_comment'></div>治化孚洽，久而益著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1282205_comment'></div>既踰年，笞箠不施，至于无讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1282205_comment'></div>相保相爱，闾里熙熙，人心敬向，日以加厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1282205_comment'></div>吏卒亦能相勉以义，视官事如其家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1282205_comment'></div>识者知其为郡有出于政刑号令之表者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1282205_comment'></div>诸司交章论荐，丞相周公必大尝遗人书，有曰：「荆门之政，于以验躬行之效」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1282205_comment'></div>三年冬十一月，语女兄曰：「先教授兄有志天下，竟不得施以没」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1282205_comment'></div>女兄衋然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1282205_comment'></div>又尝谓家人曰：「吾将死矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1282205_comment'></div>或曰：「安得此不祥语，骨肉将奈何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1282205_comment'></div>先生曰：「亦自然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1282205_comment'></div>又告僚属曰：「某将告终」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1282205_comment'></div>先生素有血疾，居旬日大作，实十二月丙午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1282205_comment'></div>越三日，疾良已，接见僚属，与论政理如平时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1282205_comment'></div>晏息静室，命扫洒焚香，家事一不挂齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1282205_comment'></div>庚戌祷雪，辛亥雪骤降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1282205_comment'></div>命具浴，浴罢，尽易新衣，幅巾端坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1282205_comment'></div>家人进药，先生却之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1282205_comment'></div>自是不复言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1282205_comment'></div>癸丑日中，奄然而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1282205_comment'></div>郡属棺敛竭诚，哭，哀甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1282205_comment'></div>吏民哭奠，充塞衢道，各有辞以叙陈痛恋之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1282205_comment'></div>柩归，门人奔哭会葬以千数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1282205_comment'></div>郡县于其讲学地为立祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1282205_comment'></div>先生遗文，诸生已次第编纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1282205_comment'></div>先生生于绍兴九年二月乙亥，享年五十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1282205_comment'></div>娶吴氏，封孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1282205_comment'></div>二子：持之，循之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1282205_comment'></div>女一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1282205_comment'></div>明年十有一月壬申葬于乡之永兴寺山，距妣饶氏孺人墓为近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1282205_comment'></div>先生之道至矣大矣，某安得而知之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1282205_comment'></div>惟某主富阳簿时摄事临安府中，始承教于先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1282205_comment'></div>及反富阳，又获从容侍诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1282205_comment'></div>偶一夕，某发本心之问，先生举是日扇讼是非以答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1282205_comment'></div>某忽省此心之清明，忽省此心之无始末，忽省此心之无所不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1282205_comment'></div>某虽凡下，不足以识先生，而于是亦知先生之心非口说所能赞述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1282205_comment'></div>所略可得而言者：日月之明，先生之明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1282205_comment'></div>四时之变化，先生之变化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1282205_comment'></div>天地之广大，先生之广大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1282205_comment'></div>鬼神之不可测，先生之不可测也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1282205_comment'></div>欲尽言之，虽穷万古不可得而尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1282205_comment'></div>虽然，先生之心与万古之人心一贯无二致，学者不可自弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1282205_comment'></div>绍熙五年二月十有六日，门人奉议郎、知饶州乐平县、主管劝农公事杨某状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_220_1282205_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年8月</a>　是月，楼钥荐公于朝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　新饶娥庙碣而记。作品：《记》？<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱未说明记文名称。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　祀饶娥仙，有文。作品：《祀饶娥仙圣文》<div id='poem_1282272' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282272' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282272?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭饶娥仙圣文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282272")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282272'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282272'>至孝格天，龙震于渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282272_comment'></div>天犹敬之，宜世称贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282272_comment'></div>是庙是享，是崇是仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282272_comment'></div>孝人所同，同知所尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282272_comment'></div>某长斯邑，首访而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282272_comment'></div>虽无旧文，当启新仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282272_comment'></div>一献为礼，神岂需此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282272_comment'></div>昭明孝道，庸示百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282272_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1282272_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　撰《孚惠王庙记》，姑系于此。<div id='poem_1282174' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282174' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282174?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乐平孚惠庙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282174")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282174_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282174'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282174'>吾邑之所崇敬，旱能致雨，祷焉而应，灵感著闻，遐迩毕趣者，曰鸣山之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282174_comment'></div>神之号曰威惠善济广祐忠烈王，宜刻石昭纪事节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282174_comment'></div>而宣和四年县尉沃彦所书，号止「威惠」，爵止「公」，使观者惑焉，不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282174_comment'></div>谨按元符三年赐庙号孚惠，崇宁四年封广利侯，宣和三年封威惠公，建炎三年封威惠王，四年加号善济，绍兴二十一年加广祐，三十年加忠烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282174_comment'></div>庙本于信之贵溪自鸣山，乐平实为旁邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282174_comment'></div>邑民诣其祠致祷者众，乃奉香火归于县治之西南二十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282174_comment'></div>亦有山焉，高倚如屏，洎水东至，拱揖其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282174_comment'></div>于是建祠，不忘其本，宜亦曰自鸣山，声传浸讹，唯曰鸣山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282174_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282174_comment'></div>神之所以灵者，以能弱冠起兵，报不共戴天之雠，追牛昌隐至贵溪祠所，杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282174_comment'></div>兵至之日，风烈云涌，水泉腾跃，山谷自鸣，故遂以此名山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282174_comment'></div>自此祠而祝之，神应无方，威灵累著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282174_comment'></div>当旱霈泽，感应如响，变化飞击，荡攘剧寇，异迹阴功，莫可殚述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282174_comment'></div>神何修而得？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282174_comment'></div>此神心至孝，痛切勇决，宁死无生，必杀昌隐，不顾利害，一心无他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282174_comment'></div>斯乃道心，斯即天地之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282174_comment'></div>《孝经》曰：「孝弟之至，通于神明，光于四海，无所不通」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282174_comment'></div>顺用而无差，顺行而无为，可以范围天地，可以发育万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282174_comment'></div>神之所自有也，不可思也，不可赞也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1282174_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　删订《己易》,姑系于此。<div id='poem_1282129' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282129' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282129?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己易</a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282129")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282129_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282129'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282129'>易者己也，非有他也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282129_comment'></div>以易为书，不以易为己，不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282129_comment'></div>以易为天地之变化，不以易为己之变化，不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282129_comment'></div>天地，我之天地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282129_comment'></div>变化，我之变化，非他物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282129_comment'></div>私者裂之，私者自小也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282129_comment'></div>包牺氏欲形容易，是已不可得，画而为━。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282129_comment'></div>于戏，是可以形容吾体之似矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282129_comment'></div>又谓是虽足以形容吾体，而吾体之中又有变化之殊焉，又无以形容之，画而为⚋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282129_comment'></div>━者，吾之也━。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282129_comment'></div>━者，吾之⚋也，可画而不可言也，可以默识而不可以智知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282129_comment'></div>━者，吾之全也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282129_comment'></div>⚋者，吾之分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282129_comment'></div>全即分也，分即全也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282129_comment'></div>自生民以来，未有能识吾之全者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282129_comment'></div>唯睹夫苍苍而清明、而在上，始能言者，名之曰天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282129_comment'></div>又睹夫隤然而博厚、而在下，又名之曰地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282129_comment'></div>清明者，吾之清明，博厚者，吾之博厚，而人不自知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282129_comment'></div>人不自知，而相与指名曰彼天也，彼地也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282129_comment'></div>如不自知其为我之手足，而曰彼手也，彼足也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282129_comment'></div>如不自知其为己之耳目鼻口，而曰彼耳目也，彼鼻口也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282129_comment'></div>是无惑乎自生民以来面墙者比比，而不如是昏之甚者，见谓聪明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282129_comment'></div>夫所以为我者，毋曰血气形貌而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282129_comment'></div>吾性澄然清明而非物，吾性洞然无际而非量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282129_comment'></div>天者，吾性中之象；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282129_comment'></div>地者，吾性中之形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282129_comment'></div>故曰「在天成象，在地成形」，皆我之所为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282129_comment'></div>混融无内外，贯通无异殊，观━画，其旨昭昭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282129_comment'></div>厥后又系之辞曰《乾》，乾，健也，言乎千变万化，不可纪极，往古来今，无所终穷，而吾体之刚健未始有改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282129_comment'></div>言乎可指之象，则所谓天者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282129_comment'></div>天即乾健者也，天即━画之所似者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282129_comment'></div>天即己也，天即易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282129_comment'></div>地者，天中之有形者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1282129_comment'></div>吾之血气形骸乃清浊阴阳之气合而成之者也，吾未见夫天与地与人之有三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1282129_comment'></div>三者形也，一者性也，亦曰道也，又曰易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1282129_comment'></div>名言之不同，而其实一体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1282129_comment'></div>故夫《乾·彖》之言，举万物之流形变化皆在其中，而六十四卦之义尽备于《乾》之一卦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1282129_comment'></div>自清浊分，人物生，男女形，万物之在天下，未尝不两，曰天与地，曰昼与夜，曰夫与妇，曰君与臣，曰尊与卑，曰大与小，曰贵与贱，曰刚与柔，曰动与静，曰善与恶，曰进与退，曰实与虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1282129_comment'></div>博观纵观，何者非两？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1282129_comment'></div>⚋者，所以象此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1282129_comment'></div>又系之辞曰《坤》，坤，顺也，明乎地与妻、与臣、与柔之类也，然非有二道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1282129_comment'></div>《坤》者两画之《乾》，《乾》者━画之坤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1282129_comment'></div>故曰：「天地之道，其为物不贰，则其生物不测」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1282129_comment'></div>又曰：「明此以南面，尧之所以为君也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1282129_comment'></div>明此以北面，舜之所以为臣也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1282129_comment'></div>又曰：「吾道一以贯之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1282129_comment'></div>则夫《乾》、《坤》之《彖》虽有「大哉」、「至哉」之辨，以明君臣上下之分，而无二元也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1282129_comment'></div>《坤》爻又曰「直方大」，又曰「以大终」也，又以明「大」与「至」之无二旨，《乾》与《坤》之无二道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1282129_comment'></div>《乾》何以三━也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1282129_comment'></div>天，此物也，人，此物也，地，此物也，无二，一也，无二，己也，皆我之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1282129_comment'></div>《坤》何以三⚋也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1282129_comment'></div>天有阴阳日月明晦也，地有刚柔高下流止也，人有君臣夫妇贵贱善恶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1282129_comment'></div>☳，天下固有如此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1282129_comment'></div>圣人系之辞曰《震》，明乎如此者阳为主，自下而动且起也，此我之变态也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1282129_comment'></div>☴，天下固有如此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1282129_comment'></div>圣人系之辞曰《巽》，明乎如此者阴为主，阴入于下，柔随之类也，此又我之变态也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1282129_comment'></div>☵，天下又有如此者也，圣人系之辞曰《坎》，言阳陷乎两阴之中，内阳而外阴，水之类也，此我之坎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1282129_comment'></div>☲，天下又有如此者也，圣人系之辞曰《离》，言阴柔不能以自立，丽乎两刚，又外阳而中虚，为火之类也，此我之离也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1282129_comment'></div>天下又有☶者，阳刚止截乎其上，故系之辞曰《艮》，艮止也，明乎我之止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1282129_comment'></div>天下又有☱者，阴柔发散乎其外，故系之辞曰《兑》，兑，说也，明乎我之说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1282129_comment'></div>举天地万物万化万理皆一而已矣，举天地万物万化万理皆《乾》而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1282129_comment'></div>《坤》者《乾》之两，非《乾》之外复有《坤》也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1282129_comment'></div>《震》、《巽》、《坎》《、离》、《艮》、《兑》，又《乾》之交错散殊，非《乾》之外复有此六物也，皆吾之变化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1282129_comment'></div>不以天地万物万化万理为己，而惟执耳目鼻口四肢为己，是剖吾之全体而裂取分寸之肤也，是梏于血气而自私也，自小也，非吾之躯止于六尺七尺而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1282129_comment'></div>坐井而观天，不知天之大也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1282129_comment'></div>坐血气而观己，不知己之广也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1282129_comment'></div>元亨利贞，吾之四德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1282129_comment'></div>吾本无此四者之殊，人之言之者自殊尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1282129_comment'></div>推吾之始，名之曰元，又曰仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1282129_comment'></div>言吾之通，名之曰亨，又曰礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1282129_comment'></div>言吾之利，名之曰利，又曰义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1282129_comment'></div>言吾之正，名之曰贞，又曰固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1282129_comment'></div>指吾之刚为九，指吾之柔为六，指吾之清浊为天地，指吾之《震》、《巽》为雷风，指吾之《坎》、《离》为水火，指吾之《艮》、《兑》为山泽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1282129_comment'></div>又指吾之变而化之，错而通之者为六十四卦，三百八十四爻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1282129_comment'></div>以吾之照临为日月，以吾之变通为四时，以吾之散殊于清浊之两间者为万物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1282129_comment'></div>以吾之视为目，以吾之听为耳，以吾之噬为口，以吾之臭为鼻，以吾之握为手，行为足，以吾之思虑为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1282129_comment'></div>言吾之变化云为深不可测，谓之曰神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1282129_comment'></div>言吾心之本曰性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1282129_comment'></div>言性之妙不可致诘，不可以人为加焉，曰命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1282129_comment'></div>得此谓之德，由此谓之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1282129_comment'></div>其觉谓之仁，其宜谓之义，其履谓之礼，其明谓之智，其昏谓之愚，其不实谓之伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1282129_comment'></div>其得谓之吉，其失谓之凶，其补过谓之无咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1282129_comment'></div>其忻然谓之喜，其惨然谓之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1282129_comment'></div>悔其非谓之悔，啬而小谓之吝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1282129_comment'></div>其不偏不过谓之中，其非邪谓之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1282129_comment'></div>其尽焉谓之圣，其未尽焉谓之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1282129_comment'></div>言乎其变谓之易，言乎其无所不通谓之道，言乎无二谓之一，今谓之己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1282129_comment'></div>谓之己者，亦非离乎六尺而复有妙己也，一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1282129_comment'></div>二之者，私也，梏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1282129_comment'></div>安得无私与梏者而告之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1282129_comment'></div>姑即六尺而细究之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1282129_comment'></div>目能视，所以能视者何物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1282129_comment'></div>耳能听？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1282129_comment'></div>所以能听者何物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1282129_comment'></div>口能噬，所以能噬者何物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1282129_comment'></div>鼻能臭，所以能臭者何物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1282129_comment'></div>手能运用屈信，所以能运用屈信者何物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1282129_comment'></div>足能步趋，所以能步趋者何物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1282129_comment'></div>血气能周流，所以能周流者何物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1282129_comment'></div>心能思虑，所以能思虑者何物？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1282129_comment'></div>目可见也，其视不可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1282129_comment'></div>耳可见也，其听不可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1282129_comment'></div>口可见，噬者不可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1282129_comment'></div>鼻可见，臭者不可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1282129_comment'></div>手足可见，其运动步趋者不可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1282129_comment'></div>血气可见，其使之周流者不可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1282129_comment'></div>心之为脏可见，其能思虑者不可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1282129_comment'></div>其可见者有大有小，有彼有此，有纵有横，有高有下，不可得而一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1282129_comment'></div>其不可见者不大不小，不彼不此，不纵不横，不高不下，不可得而二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1282129_comment'></div>视与听若不一，其不可见则一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1282129_comment'></div>视、听与噬、臭若不一，其不可见则一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1282129_comment'></div>运用步趋、周流思虑若不一，其不可见则一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1282129_comment'></div>是不可见者在视非视，在听非听，在噬非噬，在臭非臭，在运用屈信非运用屈信，在步趋非步趋，在周流非周流，在思虑非思虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1282129_comment'></div>视如此，听如此，噬如此，臭如此，运用如此，步趋如此，周流如此，思虑如此，不思虑亦如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1282129_comment'></div>昼如此，夜如此，寐如此，寤如此，生如此，死如此，天如此，地如此，日月如此，四时如此，鬼神如此，行如此，止如此，古如此，今如此，前如此，后如此，彼如此，此如此，万如此，一如此，圣人如此，众人如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1282129_comment'></div>自有而不自察也，终身由之而不知其道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1282129_comment'></div>为圣者不加，为愚者不损也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1282129_comment'></div>自明也，自昏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1282129_comment'></div>此未尝昏，此未尝明也，或者蔽之、二之，自以为昏、为明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1282129_comment'></div>昏则二，明则一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1282129_comment'></div>明因昏而立名，不有昏者，明无自而名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1282129_comment'></div>昏明皆人也，皆名也，非天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1282129_comment'></div>天即道，天即乾，天即易，天即人，天与人亦名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1282129_comment'></div>《大传》曰「鼓万物而不与圣人同忧」，此非先圣之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1282129_comment'></div>忧即天，万物即天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1282129_comment'></div>孔门之徒闻圣人之言而差之，以己意参其间，而有是言也，此非吾孔子之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1282129_comment'></div>「吾道一以贯之」，此孔子之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1282129_comment'></div>其曰「易与天地准」，此亦非孔子之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1282129_comment'></div>何以明之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1282129_comment'></div>天地即易也，幽明本无故，不必曰「仰观俯察」而后知其故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1282129_comment'></div>死生本无说，不必「原始要终」而后知其说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1282129_comment'></div>是皆非吾孔子之言也，其徒之己说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1282129_comment'></div>神即易，道即善，其曰「继之者善也」，离而二之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1282129_comment'></div>离道以善，庄周陷溺乎虚无之学也，非圣人之大道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1282129_comment'></div>孔子曰：「易，其至矣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1282129_comment'></div>夫易，圣人所以崇德而广业也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1282129_comment'></div>此孔子之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1282129_comment'></div>圣人即易也，德业即易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1282129_comment'></div>继曰「天地设位，而易行乎其中」，又非孔子之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1282129_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1282129_comment'></div>离易与天地而二之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1282129_comment'></div>「子曰」之下，其言多善，间有微碍者，传录纪述者之差也，其大旨则善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1282129_comment'></div>不系之「子曰」者，其言多不善，非圣人之言故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1282129_comment'></div>乾即易，坤即易，其曰：「乾坤毁，则无以见易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1282129_comment'></div>易不可见，则乾坤或几乎息」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1282129_comment'></div>又曰：「形而上者谓之道，形而下者谓之器」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1282129_comment'></div>其非圣言，断断如白黑，如一二之易辨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1282129_comment'></div>凡如此类，不可胜纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1282129_comment'></div>善学《易》者求诸己，不求诸书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1282129_comment'></div>古圣作《易》，凡以开吾心之明而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1282129_comment'></div>不求诸己而求诸书，其不明古圣之所指也甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1282129_comment'></div>是古圣指东，学者求西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1282129_comment'></div>读书者满天下，省己者千无一，万无一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1282129_comment'></div>孔氏之门学者不知其几，而日至者无几也，月至者又无几也，三月不违者颜氏子一人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1282129_comment'></div>他日子夏、子张、子游以有若似圣人矣，而况于不在孔门者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1282129_comment'></div>幸有一曾子独不然，曰：「不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1282129_comment'></div>江汉以濯之，秋阳以暴之，皓皓乎不可尚已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1282129_comment'></div>此岂训诂之所能解也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1282129_comment'></div>知之者自知也，不可以语人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1282129_comment'></div>所可得而语人者，曰「吾无行而不与二三子者」而已，终不可得而言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1282129_comment'></div>曰「吾有知乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1282129_comment'></div>无知也」而已，实无得以告人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1282129_comment'></div>何为其然也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1282129_comment'></div>尚不可得而思也，矧可得而言也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1282129_comment'></div>尚不可得而有也，矧可得而知也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1282129_comment'></div>然则昏者亦不思而遂己，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1282129_comment'></div>曰正恐不能遂己，诚遂己，则不学之良能，不虑之良知，我所自有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1282129_comment'></div>仁义礼智，我所自有也，万善自备也，百非自绝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1282129_comment'></div>意、必、固、我无自而生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1282129_comment'></div>虽尧、舜、禹、汤、文、武、周公、孔子何以异于是？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1282129_comment'></div>虽然，思亦何害于事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1282129_comment'></div>箕子曰「思」、曰「睿」，孔子曰「学而不思则罔」，周公「仰而思之，夜以继日」，思亦何害于吾事也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1282129_comment'></div>「庸言之信，庸行之谨」，不可以精粗论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1282129_comment'></div>「儆戒无虞，罔失法度」，正易道之妙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1282129_comment'></div>尧舜「允执厥中」，执此也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1282129_comment'></div>「兢兢业业」，弗敢怠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1282129_comment'></div>禹之「克艰」，不敢易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1282129_comment'></div>汤「改过不吝」，去其不善而复于善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1282129_comment'></div>文王「翼翼」，小心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1282129_comment'></div>信吾信，谨吾谨，儆戒吾儆戒，执吾执，兢兢吾兢兢，业业吾业业，艰吾艰，改吾改，翼翼吾翼翼，无二我也，无二易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1282129_comment'></div>既曰「天下何思何虑」矣，而又曰执、曰兢兢业业、曰艰、曰改过、曰翼翼，无思无虑者固如此乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1282129_comment'></div>但兢兢，但业业，但克艰而弗易，但改过，但翼翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1282129_comment'></div>方兢兢业业，克艰而不易时，此心果可得而见乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1282129_comment'></div>果不可得而见乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1282129_comment'></div>果动乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1282129_comment'></div>果不动乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1282129_comment'></div>特未之察耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1282129_comment'></div>似动而不移也，似变而未尝改也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1282129_comment'></div>不改不移，谓之寂然不动可也，谓之无思无虑可也，谓之不疾而速、不行而至可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1282129_comment'></div>此天下之至动也，此天下之至赜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1282129_comment'></div>象也者，像此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1282129_comment'></div>爻也者，效此者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1282129_comment'></div>非赜自赜，动自动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1282129_comment'></div>一物而殊名也，一人而姓名字行之不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1282129_comment'></div>此非沈虚陷寂者之所能识也，亦非憧憧往来者之所能知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1282129_comment'></div>然而至易也，至简也，或者自以为难，近取诸身，殊不远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1282129_comment'></div>身犹远尔，近取诸心，即此心而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1282129_comment'></div>曾子传之，曰：「夫子之道，忠恕而已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1282129_comment'></div>孟子学之，曰：「仁，人心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1282129_comment'></div>又曰：「恻隐之心，人皆有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1282129_comment'></div>羞恶之心，人皆有之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1282129_comment'></div>又曰：「今人乍见孺子将入于井，皆有怵惕恻隐之心，非所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_201_1282129", 1282129, "Clauses/606/Comments/0")'>内交</span>于孺子之父母也，非所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_201_1282129", 1282129, "Clauses/607/Comments/1")'>要誉</span>于乡党朋友也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1282129_comment'></div>于戏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1282129_comment'></div>此足以指明人心之本良矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1282129_comment'></div>而学者往往遂领孟子之意而不复疑其有他者，千万而不一二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1282129_comment'></div>故孟子言必称尧舜，于以知孟子之言虽谆谆，而当时之听之者多藐藐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1282129_comment'></div>此道甚明，甚易，甚简，而人自疑，自惑，不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1282129_comment'></div>使当时闻言而遂信者众，必不至劳孟子谆谆如此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1282129_comment'></div>能识恻隐之真心于孺子将入井之时，则何思何虑之妙人人之所自有也，纯诚洞白之质人人之所自有也，广大无疆之体人人之所自有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1282129_comment'></div>此心常见于日用饮食之间，造次颠沛之间，而人不自省也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1282129_comment'></div>孔子曰：「造次必于是，颠沛必于是」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1282129_comment'></div>子思曰：「道也者，不可须臾离也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1282129_comment'></div>可离，非道也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1282129_comment'></div>当曰道也者，未始须臾离也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1282129_comment'></div>非曰造次间为之，颠沛间为之，无须臾而不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1282129_comment'></div>是心本一也，无二也，无尝断而复续也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1282129_comment'></div>无向也不如是而今如是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1282129_comment'></div>无向也如是而今不如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1282129_comment'></div>昼夜一也，古今一也，少壮不强而衰老不弱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1282129_comment'></div>可强可弱者血气也，无强无弱者心也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1282129_comment'></div>有断有续者思虑也，无断无续者心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1282129_comment'></div>能明此心，则思虑有断续，而吾心无断续；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1282129_comment'></div>血气有强弱，而吾心无强弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1282129_comment'></div>有思无思而吾心无二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1282129_comment'></div>不能明此心，则以思虑为心，虽欲无断续，不可得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1282129_comment'></div>以血气为己，虽欲无强弱，不可得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1282129_comment'></div>虽欲造次于是，颠沛于是，无须臾不于是，勉强从事，不须臾而罢矣，况于造次乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1282129_comment'></div>况于颠沛乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1282129_comment'></div>《书》曰：「作德心逸日休，作伪心劳日拙」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1282129_comment'></div>如此则亦伪而已矣，非诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1282129_comment'></div>孔子曰「主忠信」，忠信者，诚实而已，无他妙也，而圣人以是为主本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1282129_comment'></div>或者过而索之，外而求之，故反失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1282129_comment'></div>忠信之心即道心，即仁义礼智之心，即不勉而中、不思而得之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1282129_comment'></div>通乎一，万事毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1282129_comment'></div>差之毫釐，缪以千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1282129_comment'></div>不远复，此心复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1282129_comment'></div>频复频放而频反也，亦危矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1282129_comment'></div>然已复，则如常矣，无咎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1282129_comment'></div>得此则吉，失此则凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1282129_comment'></div>无虞他日之吉凶，但观一念虑之得失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1282129_comment'></div>当《乾》之初而不肯潜，此心放也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1282129_comment'></div>当五而不能飞，此心固也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1282129_comment'></div>当三而不惕，此心慢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1282129_comment'></div>当四而不疑，此心止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1282129_comment'></div>循吾本心以往，则能飞，能潜，能疑，能惕，能用天下之九，亦能用天下之六，能尽通天下之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1282129_comment'></div>仕止久速，一合其宜，周旋曲折，各当其可，非勤劳而为之也，吾心中自有如是十百千万散殊之正义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1282129_comment'></div>礼仪三百，威仪三千，非吾心外物也，故曰性之德也，合内外之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1282129_comment'></div>故时措之宜也，言乎其自宜也，非求乎宜者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1282129_comment'></div>孔子曰「道不远人」，人之为道而远人，不可以为道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1282129_comment'></div>人之为道似善矣，而孔子截截断断，甚言其不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1282129_comment'></div>孟子窥之，亦曰：「人之所不学而能者，其良能也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1282129_comment'></div>所不虑而知者，其良知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1282129_comment'></div>孩提之童，无不知爱其亲者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1282129_comment'></div>及其长也，无不知敬其兄也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1282129_comment'></div>此岂计度而图之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1282129_comment'></div>此岂拟议而成之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1282129_comment'></div>「拟议而成其变化」，此非圣人之言也，学者之臆说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1282129_comment'></div>孰知夫「君子终日乾乾」而非意也，「频复独复」而非反也，「利于不息之贞」而非升也，「震来虩虩」非惧也，「其亡其亡」非虑也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1282129_comment'></div>何「天之衢亨」非通也，「括囊无咎无誉」非闭也，「三日不食」非穷也，「扬于王庭」非得志也，「介于石」非止也，「出门同人」非往也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1282129_comment'></div>吾终日用之而鬼神莫我识也，圣智莫我测也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1282129_comment'></div>虽我亦有所不自知，而况于他人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1282129_comment'></div>如秋阳之暴，至白而无瑕也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1282129_comment'></div>如江汉之濯，至洁而无滓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1282129_comment'></div>混混乎无涯无畔、无始无终也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1282129_comment'></div>天地非大也，毫发非小也，昼非明、夜非晦也，往非古也，此非今也，它日非后也，「鸢飞戾天」非鸢也，「鱼跃于渊」非鱼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1282129_comment'></div>天下被日月之明照而不知其自我也，天下沾雨露之润而不知其自我也，天下畏雷霆之威而不知其自我也，日夜行乎吾己之中而以为他物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1282129_comment'></div>其曰「范围天地，发育万物」也，非过论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1282129_comment'></div>孔子曰「哀乐相生」，虽使正明目而视之，不可得而见也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1282129_comment'></div>倾耳而听之，不可得而闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1282129_comment'></div>哀乐必有形，哭笑必有声，而曰不可见，不可闻，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1282129_comment'></div>此非心思之所能及也，非言语之所能载也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1282129_comment'></div>我之所自有也，而不可知也，不可识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1282129_comment'></div>书不尽言，言不尽意，未有知近而不知远也，未有知小而不知大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1282129_comment'></div>远近一物也，小大无二体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1282129_comment'></div>闺门之内若近而实远也，若小而实大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1282129_comment'></div>即敬即爱，无不通矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1282129_comment'></div>有伦有叙，无不同矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1282129_comment'></div>放之东海之东而准也，放之西海之西而准也，放之南海之南而准也，放之北海之北而准也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1282129_comment'></div>不可思也，不可远也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_278_1282129_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　有诗，姑系于此。作品：《游乐平明岩》<span class='inlineComment2'>（“游”，年谱误为“题”）</span>《贺王使君南风》《上耿泉使生朝云台》《上邓宪生辰岷源》<div id='poem_131303' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131303' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131303?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游乐平明岩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_131303")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_131303_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131303'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131303'>西风吹作明岩去，石屋高虚滴如乳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131303_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131303'>是谁不是洞中仙，无人自信吾为主。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131303_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131303'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_131303_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_472863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_472863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/472863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上耿泉生朝<span class='inlineComment2'>（云台寿泉使显谟太监公也）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_472863")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_472863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_472863'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_472863'>瞻彼云台，有那其武。<div id='poem_sentence_0_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_472863'>祝阿发迹，中兴元辅。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_1_472863_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_472863'>历世数十<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作卜）</span>，有孙惟良。<div id='poem_sentence_2_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_472863'>恺悌君子，之纪之纲。<span class='charType'>（二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_3_472863_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_472863'>柔亦不茹，刚亦不吐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_472863'>有志而宽，夫谁敢侮。<div id='poem_sentence_5_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_472863'>天子曰于，亟来辅予。<div id='poem_sentence_6_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_472863'>实彼周行，为上大夫。<div id='poem_sentence_7_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_472863'>乃眷西顾，畀之节符。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_8_472863_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_472863'>是司九府，爰总数路，爰究爰度。<div id='poem_sentence_9_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_472863'>阜丰化布，国用是裕。<span class='charType'>（四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_10_472863_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_472863'>江左矜刑，狱平讼清。<div id='poem_sentence_11_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_472863'>惟清惟明，民用以宁，奸宄亦惩。<span class='charType'>（五章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_12_472863_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_472863'>乃抚徽人，惠绥千里。<div id='poem_sentence_13_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_472863'>匪亟匪除，匪作匪异，而郡亦治。<span class='charType'>（六章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_14_472863_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_472863'>泉课复艰，属任斯难。<div id='poem_sentence_15_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_472863'>□□斧扆，节至累颁，公毋惮烦。<span class='charType'>（七章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_16_472863_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_472863'>洎阳为邑，实惟所临。<div id='poem_sentence_17_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_472863'>宽简虽至，威信亦深。<div id='poem_sentence_18_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_472863'>敢不兢兢，治所赋金。<div id='poem_sentence_19_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_472863'>以谨以程，以恪以忱。<span class='charType'>（八章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_20_472863_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_472863'>惟公诞弥，良月惟时。<div id='poem_sentence_21_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_472863'>地数盈成，梦维熊罴。<div id='poem_sentence_22_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_472863'>何以寿之，南山维基，松柏维滋。<div id='poem_sentence_23_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_472863'>毋祝毋祈，公自有之。<div id='poem_sentence_24_472863_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_472863'>某也作诗，于以敬之。<span class='charType'>（九章）</span><br /></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_472863_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_472864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_472864' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/472864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上邓宪生<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_472864")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_472864_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_472864_0'>① 晨岷源寿江东使者司谏邓公也乐平令杨某有祝颂之辞于诞晨以献焉</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_472864'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_472864'>维彼岷源，维深且长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_472864'>是为大江，润泽南方。<span class='charType'>（一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_1_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_472864'>维江之东，有贤使者。<div id='poem_sentence_2_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_472864'>惠德似之，溥泽润下。<span class='charType'>（二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_3_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_472864'>使者维公<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作何）</span>，有祖高密。<div id='poem_sentence_4_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_472864'>云台第一，流芳泌泌。<span class='charType'>（三章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_5_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_472864'>有孙维良，秉德正方。<div id='poem_sentence_6_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_472864'>天子曰于，寘彼周行。<span class='charType'>（四章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_7_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_472864'>古之遗直，亟辅予德。<div id='poem_sentence_8_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_472864'>疾风劲草，岁寒松柏。<span class='charType'>（五章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_9_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_472864'>乃眷西顾，金节畀之。<div id='poem_sentence_10_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_472864'>礼乐光华，亦王近畿。<span class='charType'>（六章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_11_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_472864'>钦哉祥刑，克宽克明。<div id='poem_sentence_12_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_472864'>民罹旱虐，焦劳发情。<span class='charType'>（七章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_13_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_472864'>民饥毋恐，惠泽方涌。<div id='poem_sentence_14_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_472864'>适兼郡符，民有天宠。<span class='charType'>（八章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_15_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_472864'>首白蠲租，宽博其模。<div id='poem_sentence_16_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_472864'>大公靡私，匪畏匪拘。<span class='charType'>（九章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_17_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_472864'>僵者起之，骨者肉之。<div id='poem_sentence_18_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_472864'>知几千万，父之母之。<span class='charType'>（十章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_19_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_472864'>洎阳为邑，罹旱则甚。<div id='poem_sentence_20_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_472864'>故维私邑，蒙泽亦甚。<span class='charType'>（十一章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_21_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_472864'>维公诞弥，端月维时。<div id='poem_sentence_22_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_472864'>梦维熊罴，何以寿之。<div id='poem_sentence_23_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_472864'>南山维基，大椿植之。<div id='poem_sentence_24_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_472864'>毋祝毋祈，公自有之。<div id='poem_sentence_25_472864_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_472864'>某也作颂，于以敬之。<span class='charType'>（十二章）</span><div id='poem_sentence_26_472864_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_472864'></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_472864_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　诏为国子博士，二少年大率县民随出境外，呼曰“杨父”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　洪迈有诗送行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　舒扬为其饯行。<br /></div>
