-----title
贵溪
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='eecefce48d0e496a899ead22cbe97467_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eecefce48d0e496a899ead22cbe97467");'><span id='eecefce48d0e496a899ead22cbe97467_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>，53岁</div><div id='eecefce48d0e496a899ead22cbe97467' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年11月9日</a>　奉檄往哭象山，十一月九日复会葬，有文。作品：《祖象山辞》<div id='poem_1282235' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282235' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282235?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祖象山先生辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年11月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282235")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282235_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282235'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282235'>某所以获执弟子之礼于先生门下，四方莫不闻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282235_comment'></div>某所以获执弟子之礼于先生门下，四方实未之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282235_comment'></div>岂惟四方之士未之知，虽前乎此千万世之已往，后乎此千万世之未来，盈天地两间皆高识深知之士，竭意悉虑，穷日夜之力，亦将莫知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282235_comment'></div>又岂惟尽古今与后世高识深知之士莫能知，虽某亦不能自知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282235_comment'></div>壬辰之岁，富春之簿廨双明阁之下，某问本心，先生举凌晨之扇讼是非之答实触某机，此四方之所知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282235_comment'></div>至于即扇讼之是非，乃有澄然之清，莹然之明，匪思匪为，某实有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282235_comment'></div>无今昔之间，无须臾之离，简易和平，变化云为，不疾而速，不行而至，莫知其乡，莫穷其涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282235_comment'></div>此岂惟某独有之举，天下之人皆有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282235_comment'></div>为恻隐，为羞恶，为恭敬，为是非，可以事亲，可以事君，可以事长，可以与朋友交，可以行于妻子，可以与上，可以临民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282235_comment'></div>天以是覆而高，地以是厚而卑，日月以是临照，四时以是变通，鬼神以是灵，万物以是生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282235_comment'></div>是虽可言而不可议，可省而不可思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282235_comment'></div>孔子曰：「吾有知乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282235_comment'></div>无知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282235_comment'></div>文王顺帝之则，亦自不识不知，况于某乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282235_comment'></div>况于四方之士乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282235_comment'></div>故圣人遏绝学者之意，以有意则有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282235_comment'></div>遏绝学者之必，以有必则有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282235_comment'></div>遏绝学者之固，以有固则有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282235_comment'></div>遏绝学者之我，以有我则有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282235_comment'></div>愈知愈离，愈思愈远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282235_comment'></div>道不远人，人之知道而远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282235_comment'></div>人不可以知道，不知犹远，而况于知乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282235_comment'></div>故夫先生平日之论，非学者之所知，非某之所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282235_comment'></div>虽然，先生之道亦既昭昭矣，何俟乎知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282235_comment'></div>仰观乎上，先生确然示人易矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282235_comment'></div>俯察乎下，先生隤然示人简矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282235_comment'></div>垂象著明者先生之著明，寒暑变化者先生之变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282235_comment'></div>《书》者，先生之政事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282235_comment'></div>《诗》者，先生之咏歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282235_comment'></div>《礼》者，先生之节文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282235_comment'></div>《春秋》者，先生之是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282235_comment'></div>《易》者，先生之变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282235_comment'></div>学者之所日诵，百姓之所日用，何俟乎复知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1282235_comment'></div>何俟乎复思？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1282235_comment'></div>勿思勿知，不可度思，矧可射思？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1282235_comment'></div>今先生释然而化矣，又岂学者之所知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1282235_comment'></div>某闻先生之讣，恸哭既绝而复续，续而又绝，绝而又复续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1282235_comment'></div>不敢伤生，微声竟哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1282235_comment'></div>亟欲奔赴，病质岌岌，度不可支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1282235_comment'></div>循循历时，荒政方殷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1282235_comment'></div>今也略定，气血微强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1282235_comment'></div>矧闻襄大事之有期，求檄以来，庸畅中肠之悲，一奠祖行，荐以此辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1282235_comment'></div>先生之道不可思，此哀亦不可思。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1282235_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1282235'><span class='label'>按：</span>《慈湖先生遗书》卷四。又见李伯恭《象山先生年谱》。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1282235_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　代李伯诚撰《祭象山文》<div id='poem_1282236' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282236' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282236?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李伯诚祭象山先生文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282236")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282236_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282236'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282236'>某于象山先生文安公受罔极之恩，片言顿觉，如脱桎梏，清明光大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282236_comment'></div>到于今，日用云为变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282236_comment'></div>夫人之丧，承讣后时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282236_comment'></div>今既襄奉，既祥禫矣，兹敢敬致三献之礼于文安公暨夫人几筵之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282236_comment'></div>日月迁流，斯觉未尝流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282236_comment'></div>死生虽异，斯觉未尝异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282236_comment'></div>言辞有极，斯觉无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282236_comment'></div>欲报之德，昊天罔极！</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1282236_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

金溪
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8aa66a3de6934e70915165dcc15b2c5e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8aa66a3de6934e70915165dcc15b2c5e");'><span id='8aa66a3de6934e70915165dcc15b2c5e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>，53岁</div><div id='8aa66a3de6934e70915165dcc15b2c5e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　及归自金溪，留宿本县仙乐观，有诗。作品：《慈湖遗书·留宿仙乐观》<br /></div>

-----title
奉化
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e6764eaefd8b48b79dd589c1804283cf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e6764eaefd8b48b79dd589c1804283cf");'><span id='e6764eaefd8b48b79dd589c1804283cf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>，59岁</div><div id='e6764eaefd8b48b79dd589c1804283cf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年10月</a>　奠舒元质，姑系于本月。作品：《奠舒元质辞》<div id='poem_1282245' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282245' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282245?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奠舒元质辞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1199年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282245")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282245_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282245'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282245'>承议郎杨某谨致奠于故友人元质舒兄通判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282245_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282245_comment'></div>昔孔子没，既葬，他日子夏、子张、子游以有若似圣人，欲以所事孔子事之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282245_comment'></div>夫有子能使同门诸友敛衽而师之，其贤可想而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282245_comment'></div>已而曾子独不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282245_comment'></div>曾子断断乎非好为己胜者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282245_comment'></div>裼裘之失言，出祖之失礼，速贫速朽之失旨，诸贤知之，曾子亦自知，曾子何所见于此而独异哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282245_comment'></div>皓皓之论，曾子自言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282245_comment'></div>曾子自知，他人安能尽知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282245_comment'></div>寥寥乎千载之下，知曾子者有几？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282245_comment'></div>知自信者有几？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282245_comment'></div>吾元质亦庶乎自知自信矣，而知元质者有几？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282245_comment'></div>元质岂有异乎人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282245_comment'></div>亦不过不失孔子所谓忠信之主本者而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282245_comment'></div>忠信人所自有，而自知其为主本者无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282245_comment'></div>元质之朋友则知元质矣，亦安能尽知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282245_comment'></div>新安从游之士蒙被元质之启佑，闻亦有知元质者矣，亦无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282245_comment'></div>平阳之民感元质抚字之爱，服元质恻怛之诚矣，知元质者为谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282245_comment'></div>吾乡万口一辞曰：「吾元质忠信士也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282245_comment'></div>吾乡多士知元质者亦屡见其人矣，而自万众言之，则亦无几尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282245_comment'></div>呜呼，已矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282245_comment'></div>某独念不获与元质俱终其学，俱进其发愤忘食之笃志，以缉熙于光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282245_comment'></div>呜呼，已矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282245_comment'></div>元质享某之奠，元质之心，惟某知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282245_comment'></div>呜呼元质！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282245_comment'></div>呜呼元质！</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1282245_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2596c5e82d2a4a65892af82ccc996e94_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2596c5e82d2a4a65892af82ccc996e94");'><span id='2596c5e82d2a4a65892af82ccc996e94_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1210&endYear=1210')">1210年</a>，70岁</div><div id='2596c5e82d2a4a65892af82ccc996e94' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1210&endYear=1210')">1210年</a>　奠拜半亭高祖考墓。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
温州（永嘉）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b317f38ef0ae4dc58ba72e98918f95e9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b317f38ef0ae4dc58ba72e98918f95e9");'><span id='b317f38ef0ae4dc58ba72e98918f95e9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1210&endYear=1212')">1210-1212年</a>，70-72岁</div><div id='b317f38ef0ae4dc58ba72e98918f95e9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1210&endYear=1210')">1210年</a>　移文首罢妓籍，尊敬贤士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1210&endYear=1210')">1210年11月12日</a>　蒋存诚葬于此日，为撰墓志铭。作品：《蒋秉信墓铭》<div id='poem_1282211' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282211' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282211?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蒋秉信墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉定三年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282211")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282211_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282211'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282211'>舜曰「道心」，明心即道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282211_comment'></div>动乎意，则为人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282211_comment'></div>孔子语子思曰：「心之精神是谓圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282211_comment'></div>孟子亦曰：「仁，人心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282211_comment'></div>心可言，不可思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282211_comment'></div>孔子知门弟子必多以孔子为有知，明告之曰：「吾有知乎哉，无知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282211_comment'></div>知即思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282211_comment'></div>又曰：「天下何思何虑」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282211_comment'></div>周公仰而思之，夜以继日，即思非思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282211_comment'></div>孔子「临事而惧，好谋而成」，即惧非惧，即谋非谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282211_comment'></div>如鉴之照，大小美恶，往来参错，具有而实无；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282211_comment'></div>如日月之光，万物毕照，入松穿竹，历历皎皎，而日月无思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282211_comment'></div>曾子曰「皓皓」，谓此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282211_comment'></div>「日至」非果有所至，不动乎意，澄然昭然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282211_comment'></div>一日之外，或动乎意，故曰日至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282211_comment'></div>自古到今，知道者千无一，万无一，故学者以知道为至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282211_comment'></div>圣人与人群居，不得不因人为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282211_comment'></div>「月至」亦非有所至，澄然昭然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282211_comment'></div>一月之外，或动乎意，故曰月至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282211_comment'></div>颜子三月不动乎意，故曰「三月不违仁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282211_comment'></div>某得之先兄和仲曰：「同舍蒋秉信因闻歌《朝中措》之词，而忽有觉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282211_comment'></div>某厥后屡奉秉信周旋，灼见秉信之果有觉，非学者所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282211_comment'></div>今其云亡，其子行中求言以发其幽光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282211_comment'></div>秉信之光，非幽所可间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282211_comment'></div>秉信讳存诚，自其上世居四明郡城中小湖之西南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282211_comment'></div>曾祖讳浚明，金紫光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282211_comment'></div>祖讳琚，大学谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282211_comment'></div>父讳从，儒者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282211_comment'></div>秉信幼不好弄，母滕氏钟爱之，曰：「当成大器」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282211_comment'></div>娶任氏，尽以奁具助嫁诸妹，全身布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282211_comment'></div>见人所行当于理，必赞必誉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282211_comment'></div>有违乎理，必告必戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282211_comment'></div>嘉定三年三月寝疾，故旧访问，必谢曰：「萃聚许久，今告违矣，毋笑毋讶」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1282211_comment'></div>七日而殁，实壬寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1282211_comment'></div>十有一月丙申，葬于韩溪之青嶂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1282211_comment'></div>呜呼，秉信之善，人所共知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1282211_comment'></div>秉信之心，人所未知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1282211_comment'></div>人皆有此心，多不自知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1282211_comment'></div>友人杨某书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1282211_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1210&endYear=1210')">1210年12月</a>　冬十二月，撰《乡记序》<div id='poem_1282121' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282121' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282121?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乡记序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1210年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282121")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282121_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282121'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282121'>权发遣温州杨某深信人性皆善，皆可以为尧舜，特动乎意则恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282121_comment'></div>日用平常实直之心无非大道，此固不可得而书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282121_comment'></div>今姑仿《周官》，书其敬敏任恤，书其孝友睦姻有学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282121_comment'></div>邑官之贤者与主记之贤士又能书其德行道艺，则尤其善者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282121_comment'></div>书善不书恶，其敬其审，某愿与四邑之士夫军民共由斯道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282121_comment'></div>嘉定三年冬十有二月。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1282121_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　守杨简始加甓土上。于是灌莽尤盛，刺壮城卒专修平之。杨公谓守莫先于社稷。有文。作品：《知温州到任谒社稷文》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　到任谒宣圣，有文。作品：《谒宣圣文》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　到任谒诸庙有文。作品：《到任谒诸庙文》<div id='poem_1282281' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282281' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282281?labeling=true' target='_blank'>到任谒诸庙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282281")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282281_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282281'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282281'>恭惟至神，无所不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282281_comment'></div>某假守于兹，祗见祠下，敢不即无所不通之道，以有事于尔神？</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1282281_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　在温州任，纪律严明。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　寓官置民田负其直，简追其隶责之而偿所负。势家第宅障官河，即日撤之，城中欢踊，名杨公河。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　撰《祭伯兄文》<div id='poem_1282254' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282254' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282254?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭伯兄文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282254")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282254_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282254'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282254'>介弟具位某谨以清酌羹羞祗荐于伯兄八七府君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282254_comment'></div>惟兄易箦，今既周星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282254_comment'></div>礼虽有制，而中心爱敬，日日新，又日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282254_comment'></div>兄灵清明，虽千变万化，不可度思，寂然如水之清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282254_comment'></div>岂惟某心永钦，百世之下，凡心光内明者，孰不兴敬，知嘉定之有人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282254_comment'></div>祝辞有尽，爱敬终无尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282254_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1282254_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　撰《半亭高祖墓记》<div id='poem_1282210' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282210' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282210?labeling=true' target='_blank'>半亭高祖墓记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282210")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282210_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282210'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282210'>朝请郎、权发遣温州军州兼管内劝农公事杨某字敬仲之高祖考九府君讳论，居于明州，今为庆元府之奉化县之忠义乡之半亭，殁而葬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282210_comment'></div>四子，伯与季及其子孙多环而居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282210_comment'></div>叔子无嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282210_comment'></div>仲子讳宗辅，即某之曾祖考，独徙而居鄞，故曾伯祖考及曾叔祖考之子孙从而徙焉者亦间有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282210_comment'></div>暨先大夫，始又自鄞而徙慈溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282210_comment'></div>先大夫乾道中尝命仲兄甃九府君墓，刻石为望，屋其门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282210_comment'></div>今门圮，北赴东嘉，奠拜墓下，感复兴怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282210_comment'></div>思复修兴，而食指众，新俸无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282210_comment'></div>方坎坎，忽半亭曾伯祖下族兄百六府君之子子才、子富、子祥合计协力作新门墙，邑里改观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282210_comment'></div>又族兄名居立石，使亿以书来，欲某识其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282210_comment'></div>某祗惟高祖府君本性清明无体量，广大无际畔，万善本备，不假造为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282210_comment'></div>日月运行，云雷风雨霜露，即吾高祖府君之变化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282210_comment'></div>草木林生，山川峙流，人物群居，父慈子孝，兄良弟弟，夫义妇听，长惠幼顺，即吾高祖府君之变化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282210_comment'></div>有孔子之言为證曰：「心之精神是谓圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282210_comment'></div>孟子亦道性善，此万古人心之所同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282210_comment'></div>五世介孙朝请郎、权发遣温州军州兼管内劝农事杨某不胜兴敬兴慕，以书于永嘉郡斋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1282210_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　撰《劝农文》<div id='poem_1282087' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282087' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282087?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永嘉劝农文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282087")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282087_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282087'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282087'>古者舜大圣人也，而耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282087_comment'></div>伊尹圣人也，而耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282087_comment'></div>耕者常情之所贱，君子之所敬，尤为本朝列圣之所敬，故守令皆以劝农系衔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282087_comment'></div>今争田之讼累累，岂有田而不肯耕？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282087_comment'></div>然大患有二：其一风俗好奢，故虽耕而终贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282087_comment'></div>其二风俗好争，以好争，故虽耕而终于贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282087_comment'></div>人情岂恶富而喜贫哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282087_comment'></div>风俗之所习尚，举一世皆以奢侈为美为荣，父子兄弟意向，州闾邻里意向，无不趋于奢，无不羞于俭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282087_comment'></div>今欲改奢而为俭，其势固难，但奢则坐见贫困，邻里罕能救，虽至亲亦罕能救。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282087_comment'></div>审思至此，则泛泛羞俭喜奢之浮毁誉何足顾恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282087_comment'></div>颜子箪瓢，垂芳万世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282087_comment'></div>崔烈虽富，人谓铜臭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282087_comment'></div>愿父老训谕子弟，勿循羞俭喜奢之浮毁誉，自取贫困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282087_comment'></div>颜子有负郭之田六十亩，尚箪食瓢饮，今田家未必人人有田，岂可不计度？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282087_comment'></div>孔子曰：「君子无所争」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282087_comment'></div>老子曰：「天道不争而善胜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282087_comment'></div>人情率喜争，岂以争为美德？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282087_comment'></div>私意作于中，好己胜而耻于下人，故争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282087_comment'></div>不思争则非君子，争则为小人，争则违天道，上帝所不与，祸灾随之，故好争者多败家遭刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282087_comment'></div>愿父老训谕子弟切勿争，败家遭刑，自取贫困，自陷于小人之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282087_comment'></div>戒之戒之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282087_comment'></div>小人以求己胜为荣，君子以求己胜为辱，以求己胜者小人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282087_comment'></div>「天道亏盈而益谦，人道恶盈而好谦，鬼神害盈而福谦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282087_comment'></div>谦即不争，谦反尊而光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282087_comment'></div>今不与尊光而取亏害，利害甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282087_comment'></div>愿父老从容暇日，审思详虑，与子弟共议，切勿以奢为荣，当以颜子箪瓢为荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282087_comment'></div>切勿以好争为荣，当以不争退逊为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282087_comment'></div>勿以老太守谆谆为虚文非真情，此实老太守爱汝辈切至之实情。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1282087_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　更永嘉郡治堂亭名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　更永嘉郡学养源堂曰永堂。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　撰《平阳阴均隄记》<div id='poem_1282186' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282186' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282186?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永嘉平阳阴均堤记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282186")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282186_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282186'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282186'>天府府庠林子君雅合平阳东西、金舟、亲仁四乡父老而下衔哀兴敬，以请于州守杨某曰：「四乡农田北距大海，西枕长江，凡四十万馀亩，被咸潮巨害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282186_comment'></div>自有江以来至于今，繇水利不治，岁告饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282186_comment'></div>嘉定元年汪令君惠抚吾邑，深虑熟计，建埭八十丈于阴均，障海潮，潴清流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282186_comment'></div>又造石门于山之麓，以时启闭，以防涨溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282186_comment'></div>给资粮佐工费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282186_comment'></div>又经理其旁之涂地，以为社仓，仿晦翁待制，奏请赈贷平阳十乡细民，不计息，遇饥岁并蠲其本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282186_comment'></div>君雅暨父老而下受汪令君无穷大恩，今承讣，巷哭路吊，念无以仰酬汪令君不报之德，今将立石阴均，刻曰『令君汪公遗爱恩波』，使十乡之民世世子孙无忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282186_comment'></div>君雅等深知使君好善乐义，敢求亲墨大书八字，并专纪其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282186_comment'></div>乞鉴四乡同欲之请，伸四乡终身悲郁之思」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282186_comment'></div>某于是乎恻然为之书且记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1282186_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　撰《陈规守城录序》<div id='poem_1282120' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282120' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282120?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈规守城录序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282120")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282120_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282120'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282120'>古志曰：天子守在四夷，天子卑守在诸侯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282120_comment'></div>诸侯守在四邻，诸侯卑守在四境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282120_comment'></div>此道甚易知，甚易行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282120_comment'></div>而自孔子殁，孔子之徒又殁，而士大夫率莫之思，莫之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282120_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282120_comment'></div>人非木石，我爱彼，彼如何不我爱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282120_comment'></div>我敬彼，彼如何不我敬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282120_comment'></div>即可使如一家，四海之内皆吾赤子，何忍取赤子而杀之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282120_comment'></div>然事有本末，法关盛衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282120_comment'></div>某有志于武备踰四十年，前数年始得陈规《守城录》，其言条理至详，某于是于守备顿省怀虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282120_comment'></div>待制陈公初镂版于九江，今士大夫罕见此书，见亦未必以为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282120_comment'></div>待制知某爱此书，取诸九江以纳东嘉郡库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282120_comment'></div>某即命多为帙，将以分遗士夫，以广国家武备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282120_comment'></div>又虑观者不本于四夷之守，不得已，故书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1282120_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年12月</a>　是月，志邹元祥墓碣。作品：《邹元祥墓碣》<div id='poem_1282214' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282214' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282214?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邹元祥墓碣</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉定四年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282214")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282214_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282214'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282214'>饶之乐平邹梦遇字元祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282214_comment'></div>四明杨某之宰乐平也，梦遇与乡贡，自是相与从容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282214_comment'></div>后某以职事至兰若，梦遇见次，言近觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282214_comment'></div>某叩之，知其觉矣，而犹不无阻，随通之，自是益澄明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282214_comment'></div>后又得梦遇之叔祖近仁字鲁卿，与之语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282214_comment'></div>厥明再语，而顿觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282214_comment'></div>末得比邑馀干之曹夙字叔达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282214_comment'></div>叔达留县庠，昼忘食，夜忘寝，旬有四五日而忽觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282214_comment'></div>呜呼，盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282214_comment'></div>自孔子殁，学者率陷溺于文辞论议，丧其本灵而事意说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282214_comment'></div>寥寥二千载，其自知自信者有几？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282214_comment'></div>若三子者可谓自知自信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282214_comment'></div>孔子曰：「心之精神是谓圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282214_comment'></div>人皆有是心，百姓日用而不知，三子知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282214_comment'></div>鲁卿之子曾字伯传，比年亦觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282214_comment'></div>呜呼，盛矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1282214_comment'></div>元祥事亲至孝，笃爱诸弟，尝语人曰：「事亲从兄之际，不思不勉，无非实地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1282214_comment'></div>变化云为，弛张阖辟，宇宙在吾手」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1282214_comment'></div>又曰：「浑然之中，品节条理粲然以列」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1282214_comment'></div>又曰：「人皆以兀坐端默为静，吾独以步趋应酬为静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1282214_comment'></div>人皆以步趋应酬为动，吾独以兀坐端默为动」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1282214_comment'></div>其舅谓元祥色温言约，神定气和，喜愠不形，动容周旋，庄肃閒泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1282214_comment'></div>其处事一于义理，不可夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1282214_comment'></div>别后进德，厥效乃尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1282214_comment'></div>久欲来见，嘉定四年春赴礼闱，罢而疾作，不可来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1282214_comment'></div>归而略平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1282214_comment'></div>孟夏三日，命二子扶坐艮斋，自谓气虽微而神则嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1282214_comment'></div>时斋明，喜甚，哦曰：「嘉木扶疏兮鸟鸣关关，暑风舒徐兮庭中閒閒，起视天宇兮浩乎虚澄」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1282214_comment'></div>还中堂，与家人茗饮罢，就寝而殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1282214_comment'></div>讣至永嘉，哭于燕堂，遣奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1282214_comment'></div>腊月，其子自得使弟自厚来，某对哭，自厚再拜：「葬有日，请志其墓」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1282214_comment'></div>铭之曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1282214'>人心至灵，自通自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1282214_comment'></div>元祥无能有所增，惟不动乎意，不昏其本灵。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1282214_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1211&endYear=1211')">1211年</a>　有文，姑系于本年。作品：《诸庙祈雨文》《祭社稷文》《奉安圣水文》《祭海神祠山文》《永嘉季春祈雨碧玉醮青词后雨作改用文》《禳火青词》《上元设醮青词》<div id='poem_1282291' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282291' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282291?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诸庙祈雨文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282291")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282291_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282291'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282291'>某兹以愆阳为灾，阖郡危惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282291_comment'></div>众祷虔虔，应亦累累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282291_comment'></div>檐溜已鸣，忽复告止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282291_comment'></div>农事甚急，过此无及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282291_comment'></div>某德未纯，某知罪矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282291_comment'></div>惟神敷惠千里之氓，锡以三日之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282291_comment'></div>生死骨肉，判于旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282291_comment'></div>某不胜恳恳祷祷之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1282291_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1282288' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282288' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282288?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祀社稷文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282288")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282288_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282288'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282288'>某以凉德，受此民社，而适愆阳，靡神不宗，蒙降霈泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282288_comment'></div>惟神无名无方，无为无疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282288_comment'></div>化生顺行，百谷用成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282288_comment'></div>兹举尝祀，尚惟神之灵雨旸以时，以迄于三登。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1282288_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1282292' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282292' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282292?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉安圣水文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282292")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282292_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282292'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282292'>某兹迎圣泽，阖郡危惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282292_comment'></div>伏惟神龙，察此切诚，悯此无告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282292_comment'></div>神气风霆，变化顷刻，锡以滂然之霖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282292_comment'></div>某曷胜恳恳祷祷、颙颙徯徯之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1282292_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1282293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>海神祠山文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282293")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282293'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282293'>天人一致，何所不通？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282293_comment'></div>人违乎天，始不一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282293_comment'></div>腹脏生疾，头目作楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282293_comment'></div>某德未纯，政事愆违，故雨旸亦愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282293_comment'></div>惟神兴慈，运神机，霈膏泽，惠我有秋，使四邑赤子不失乳哺，护养本有之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282293_comment'></div>某不胜恳祷颙徯之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1282293_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1282306' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282306' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282306?labeling=true' target='_blank'>永嘉季春祈雨碧玉醮青词后雨作改用</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282306")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282306_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282306'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282306'>三才一致，人自愆违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282306_comment'></div>久旱众忧，兹焉贡祷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282306_comment'></div>累蒙应矣，未至霶然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282306_comment'></div>仰碧玉之垂慈，悯苍生之无告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282306_comment'></div>赦臣知罪之故，取民迁善之新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282306_comment'></div>启醮初筵，日庚申而奏请；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282306_comment'></div>夬泽终夕，夜甲乙而如倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282306_comment'></div>四邑欢呼，拜生死骨肉之大赐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282306_comment'></div>九天变化，妙云行施雨之神功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282306_comment'></div>更祈三日已往之霖，卒济百谷时播之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282306_comment'></div>臣无任至感至祷激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1282306_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1282301' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282301' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282301?labeling=true' target='_blank'>禳火青词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282301")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282301_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282301'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282301'>臣钦惟上天不可以言而格，惟善可以格，温民改过迁善者寖多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282301_comment'></div>臣德未纯，不敢荒怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282301_comment'></div>惟上帝悯斯护斯，保养而扶持之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282301_comment'></div>俾毋罹其灾，拂乱其所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282301_comment'></div>帝心融明，有感斯应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282301_comment'></div>祷斯叩斯，不可度斯。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1282301_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1282299' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282299' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282299?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上元设醮青词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1211年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282299")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282299_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282299'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282299'>敬以惟皇上帝，无思无为，无所不在，无所不照知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282299_comment'></div>有感斯应，不可度思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282299_comment'></div>帝降衷于民，民皆有无思无为，无所不照知之常性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282299_comment'></div>惟日用不自知，私欲繁兴，祸灾随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282299_comment'></div>某虽微觉，未精未一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282299_comment'></div>谬当郡寄，政理阙失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282299_comment'></div>回禄之祸灾由人兴，匪天降之灾，咸自取之，臣不敢不勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282299_comment'></div>惟帝兴慈，悯斯宥斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282299_comment'></div>民在涂炭，如切臣之肌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282299_comment'></div>惟帝兴慈，悯斯宥斯！</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1282299_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1212&endYear=1212')">1212年</a>　在温州，先生仪典旷绝，邦人创见之，莫不瞿然竦观，屛息立。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1212&endYear=1212')">1212年</a>　简在郡廉俭自将，奉养菲薄。闾巷雍睦，无忿争声，民爱之如父母，咸画像祀之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1212&endYear=1212')">1212年</a>　先生荐戴蒙于朝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1212&endYear=1212')">1212年</a>　与周坦、薛疑之、汤建交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1212&endYear=1212')">1212年</a>　赠陈伯量书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1212&endYear=1212')">1212年</a>　与徐凤交，姑系于本年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1212&endYear=1212')">1212年</a>　迁驾部员外郞，老稚扶携缘道，倾城哭送。<br /></div>

-----title
苏州（吴县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fa64127501d94fba96a8a61e307f147d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fa64127501d94fba96a8a61e307f147d");'><span id='fa64127501d94fba96a8a61e307f147d_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1218&endYear=1218')">1218年</a>　有诗示叶元吉，姑系于本年。作品：《示叶元吉》<div id='poem_131223' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131223' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131223?labeling=true' target='_blank'>示叶元吉</a><span class='authorDate'>（1218年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_131223")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_131223_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131223'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131223'>元吉三更非鼓声，慈湖一夜听鹅鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131223_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131223'>是同是异难声说，何虑何思自混成。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131223_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131223'>炉炭几番来暖热，天窗一点吐圆明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131223_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131223'>起来又睹无穷景，水槛澄光万里清。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131223_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131223'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131223_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1218&endYear=1218')">1218年</a>　有文，姑系于本年。作品：《叶元吉请书》<div id='poem_1282110' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282110' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282110?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叶元吉请书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1218年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282110")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282110_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282110'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282110'>皋陶曰：「兢兢业业」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282110_comment'></div>孔子「发愤忘食」，「为之不厌」，又曰：「造次必于是，颠沛必于是」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1282110_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1218&endYear=1218')">1218年</a>　与张端义交，姑系于本年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1218&endYear=1218')">1218年</a>　有文，姑系于本年。作品：《吴县讲义》<div id='poem_1282128' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1282128' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1282128?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴学讲义</a><span class='authorDate'>（1218年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_1282128")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1282128_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1282128'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1282128'>人心自正，人心自善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1282128_comment'></div>孩提之童无不知爱其亲，及长，无不知敬其兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1282128_comment'></div>不学而能，不虑而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1282128_comment'></div>人皆有恻隐之心，皆有羞恶之心，皆有恭敬之心，皆有是非之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1282128_comment'></div>孔子语子思曰：「心之精神是谓圣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1282128_comment'></div>人人皆与尧、舜、禹、汤、文、武、周公、孔子同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1282128_comment'></div>人心非血气，非形体，精神广大无际畔，范围天地，发育万物，何独圣人有之，人皆有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1282128_comment'></div>时有古今，道无古今；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1282128_comment'></div>形有古今，心无古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1282128_comment'></div>百姓日用此心之妙而不自知，以其意动而有过，故不自知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1282128_comment'></div>孔子曰：「改而止」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1282128_comment'></div>谓学者改过即止，无外起意，无适无莫，蒙以养之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1282128_comment'></div>孔子曰：「吾有知乎哉，无知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1282128_comment'></div>文王「不识不知」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1282128_comment'></div>孔子每每戒学者毋意，意态有四：必、固、我，皆意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1282128_comment'></div>如蒙如愚，以养其正，作圣之功。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1282128_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1218&endYear=1218')">1218年</a>　有诗题平江府泰伯庙，姑系于本年。作品：《谒泰伯庙》<div id='poem_131301' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_131301' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/131301?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒泰伯庙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1218年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28632, "南宋", "杨简", "poem_title_131301")'>杨简</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_131301_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_131301'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_131301'>三以天下让，先圣谓至德。<div id='poem_sentence_0_131301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_131301'>某也拜庙下，太息复太息。<div id='poem_sentence_1_131301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_131301'>三辞不难知，泰伯无人识。<div id='poem_sentence_2_131301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_131301'>胡为无得称，万象妙无极<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_131301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_131301'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_131301_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_131301'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_131301_0'>⑴ 或曰泰伯之神无形体何故言象又曰万通大道者匪有匪无象即无万即一一即万尚不可思而可言乎即无言天地内外皆泰伯人实见之而不识</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_131301_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
